<script>
// ── Theme ──
(function() {
  var saved = localStorage.getItem('kt-theme');
  if (saved === 'light') document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
  updateThemeUI();
})();
function toggleTheme() {
  var html = document.documentElement;
  var isLight = html.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light';
  if (isLight) { html.removeAttribute('data-theme'); localStorage.setItem('kt-theme', 'dark'); }
  else { html.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light'); localStorage.setItem('kt-theme', 'light'); }
  updateThemeUI();
  mermaid.initialize({
    startOnLoad: false,
    theme: document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? 'default' : 'dark',
    securityLevel: 'loose',
    fontFamily: '-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Segoe UI, sans-serif'
  });
  if (chart && treeData) renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
}
function updateThemeUI() {
  var isLight = document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light';
  document.getElementById('themeIcon').textContent = isLight ? '☀️' : '🌙';
  document.getElementById('themeLabel').textContent = isLight ? 'Light' : 'Dark';
}
function getTooltipColors() {
  var isLight = document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light';
  return isLight
    ? { bg: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.98)', text: '#1a1a2e', meta: '#6b7280', title: '#4f46e5', body: '#4a4a6a', divider: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.12)', keywordBg: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.08)', keywordColor: '#4f46e5', label: '#1a1a2e', leafLabel: '#6b7280' }
    : { bg: 'rgba(15,17,23,0.96)', text: '#e4e4e7', meta: '#71717a', title: '#818cf8', body: '#a1a1aa', divider: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.15)', keywordBg: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.12)', keywordColor: '#818cf8', label: '#e4e4e7', leafLabel: '#a1a1aa' };
}
function getChartLabelColor() {
  return document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? '#1a1a2e' : '#e4e4e7';
}
function getChartLeafLabelColor() {
  return document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? '#6b7280' : '#a1a1aa';
}

// ── Mermaid Init ──
mermaid.initialize({
  startOnLoad: false,
  theme: document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? 'default' : 'dark',
  securityLevel: 'loose',
  fontFamily: '-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Segoe UI, sans-serif'
});

let chart = null;
let treeData = null;
let allNodes = [];
let currentLayout = 'LR';
let currentExpandLevel = 2;
let widthSpacing = 100;
let heightSpacing = 100;
const SPACING_MIN = 20;
const SPACING_MAX = 300;
let searchExpanded = false;

// Edit state
let editState = {
  active: false,
  nodeData: null,
  inputEl: null
};
let currentDisplayNode = null;
const API_BASE = window.location.port === '8700' ? '' : 'http://localhost:8700';

// Level color palette
const LEVEL_COLORS = [
  '#6366f1', '#818cf8', '#22c55e', '#eab308', '#f97316', '#a78bfa'
];

function getNodeColor(level) {
  return LEVEL_COLORS[Math.min(level, LEVEL_COLORS.length - 1)];
}

function formatSummary(summary, keywords, maxLen) {
  if (!summary) return '';
  var text = summary;
  if (maxLen > 0 && text.length > maxLen) {
    text = text.substring(0, maxLen) + '…';
  }
  var sentences = text.split(/(?<=[。；])/);
  var groupSize = 3;
  var html = '';
  for (var i = 0; i < sentences.length; i += groupSize) {
    var chunk = sentences.slice(i, i + groupSize).join('');
    if (keywords && keywords.length > 0) {
      keywords.forEach(function(kw) {
        if (kw.length >= 2) {
          var escaped = kw.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
          var regex = new RegExp('(' + escaped + ')', 'g');
          chunk = chunk.replace(regex, '<span class="sum-hl">$1</span>');
        }
      });
    }
    html += '<p class="sum-para">' + chunk + '</p>';
  }
  return html;
}

function escapeHtml(text) {
  return text.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
}

function highlightKeywords(text, keywords) {
  if (!keywords || keywords.length === 0) return text;
  var result = text;
  keywords.forEach(function(kw) {
    if (kw.length >= 2) {
      var escaped = kw.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
      var regex = new RegExp('(' + escaped + ')', 'g');
      result = result.replace(regex, '<span class="sum-hl">$1</span>');
    }
  });
  return result;
}

function renderInlineFormulas(text) {
  text = text.replace(/\$\$(.+?)\$\$/g, '<span class="inline-formula" data-formula="$$$1$$">$$1$$</span>');
  text = text.replace(/(?<!\$)\$(?!\$)(.+?)(?<!\$)\$(?!\$)/g,
    '<span class="inline-formula" data-formula="$$$1$">$$1$</span>');
  return text;
}

function renderMarkdownTable(tableLines, keywords) {
  if (tableLines.length < 2) return '';
  var headerCells = tableLines[0].split('|').filter(function(c) { return c.trim() !== ''; });
  var dataStart = 1;
  if (tableLines.length > 1 && /^[\s|:-]+$/.test(tableLines[1])) {
    dataStart = 2;
  }
  var html = '<div class="table-wrapper"><table class="md-table"><thead><tr>';
  headerCells.forEach(function(cell) {
    html += '<th>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.trim()), keywords) + '</th>';
  });
  html += '</tr></thead><tbody>';
  for (var r = dataStart; r < tableLines.length; r++) {
    var cells = tableLines[r].split('|').filter(function(c) { return c.trim() !== ''; });
    html += '<tr>';
    cells.forEach(function(cell) {
      html += '<td>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.trim()), keywords) + '</td>';
    });
    html += '</tr>';
  }
  html += '</tbody></table></div>';
  return html;
}

function renderHtmlTable(htmlString, keywords) {
  try {
    var parser = new DOMParser();
    var doc = parser.parseFromString(htmlString, 'text/html');
    var table = doc.querySelector('table');
    if (!table) return escapeHtml(htmlString);
    var rows = table.querySelectorAll('tr');
    if (rows.length === 0) return '';
    var html = '<div class="table-wrapper"><table class="md-table">';
    var firstRowCells = rows[0].querySelectorAll('td, th');
    var hasHead = table.querySelector('thead') || (firstRowCells.length > 0 && firstRowCells[0].tagName === 'TH');
    var startRow = 0;
    if (hasHead) {
      html += '<thead><tr>';
      firstRowCells.forEach(function(cell) {
        var colspan = cell.getAttribute('colspan') || 1;
        var rowspan = cell.getAttribute('rowspan') || 1;
        html += '<th' + (colspan > 1 ? ' colspan="' + colspan + '"' : '')
             + (rowspan > 1 ? ' rowspan="' + rowspan + '"' : '')
             + '>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.textContent.trim()), keywords) + '</th>';
      });
      html += '</tr></thead><tbody>';
      startRow = 1;
    } else {
      html += '<tbody>';
    }
    for (var r = startRow; r < rows.length; r++) {
      html += '<tr>';
      var cells = rows[r].querySelectorAll('td, th');
      cells.forEach(function(cell) {
        var colspan = cell.getAttribute('colspan') || 1;
        var rowspan = cell.getAttribute('rowspan') || 1;
        html += '<td' + (colspan > 1 ? ' colspan="' + colspan + '"' : '')
             + (rowspan > 1 ? ' rowspan="' + rowspan + '"' : '')
             + '>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.textContent.trim()), keywords) + '</td>';
      });
      html += '</tr>';
    }
    html += '</tbody></table></div>';
    return html;
  } catch(e) {
    return escapeHtml(htmlString);
  }
}

function renderNodeMermaid(mermaidCode, containerId) {
  if (!mermaidCode) return '';
  return '<div class="field-label">Flowchart</div>'
    + '<div class="mermaid-block" data-mermaid-id="' + containerId + '">'
    + '<pre class="mermaid-source" style="display:none;">' + escapeHtml(mermaidCode) + '</pre>'
    + '<div class="mermaid-render" id="' + containerId + '"></div></div>';
}

function renderNodeTables(tables) {
  if (!tables || tables.length === 0) return '';
  var html = '<div class="field-label">Tables</div>';
  tables.forEach(function(tableStr) {
    var tableLines = tableStr.split('\n').filter(function(l) { return l.trim(); });
    html += renderMarkdownTable(tableLines, []);
  });
  return html;
}

async function postRenderMathAndMermaid(container) {
  if (typeof renderMathInElement === 'function') {
    renderMathInElement(container, {
      delimiters: [
        { left: '$$', right: '$$', display: true },
        { left: '$', right: '$', display: false },
        { left: '\\(', right: '\\)', display: false },
        { left: '\\[', right: '\\]', display: true }
      ],
      throwOnError: false
    });
  }
  var mermaidBlocks = container.querySelectorAll('.mermaid-block');
  for (var block of mermaidBlocks) {
    var sourceEl = block.querySelector('.mermaid-source');
    var renderEl = block.querySelector('.mermaid-render');
    if (sourceEl && renderEl && !renderEl.getAttribute('data-processed')) {
      var code = sourceEl.textContent.trim();
      if (code) {
        try {
          var id = renderEl.id || ('mermaid-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9));
          var result = await mermaid.render(id + '-svg', code);
          renderEl.innerHTML = result.svg;
          renderEl.setAttribute('data-processed', 'true');
        } catch (e) {
          renderEl.innerHTML = '<pre style="color:var(--red);font-size:11px;">Mermaid error: '
            + escapeHtml(e.message || String(e)) + '</pre>';
          renderEl.setAttribute('data-processed', 'true');
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

var _mermaidCounter = 0;
function formatContent(text, keywords, maxLen) {
  if (!text) return '';
  var t = text;
  if (maxLen > 0 && t.length > maxLen) {
    t = t.substring(0, maxLen) + '…';
  }
  var lines = t.split('\n');
  var html = '';
  var i = 0;
  while (i < lines.length) {
    var line = lines[i].trim();
    if (!line) { i++; continue; }
    if (line.startsWith('```mermaid')) {
      var mermaidLines = [];
      i++;
      while (i < lines.length && lines[i].trim() !== '```') {
        mermaidLines.push(lines[i]);
        i++;
      }
      if (i < lines.length) i++;
      var mermaidCode = mermaidLines.join('\n').trim();
      if (mermaidCode) {
        _mermaidCounter++;
        var mermaidId = 'mermaid-inline-' + _mermaidCounter + '-' + Date.now();
        html += '<div class="mermaid-block" data-mermaid-id="' + mermaidId + '">'
             + '<pre class="mermaid-source" style="display:none;">' + escapeHtml(mermaidCode) + '</pre>'
             + '<div class="mermaid-render" id="' + mermaidId + '"></div></div>';
      }
      continue;
    }
    if (line.startsWith('|') && line.endsWith('|')) {
      var tableLines = [];
      while (i < lines.length && lines[i].trim().startsWith('|') && lines[i].trim().endsWith('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[i].trim());
        i++;
      }
      html += renderMarkdownTable(tableLines, keywords);
      continue;
    }
    if (line.toLowerCase().startsWith('<table')) {
      var tableHtml = line;
      if (!line.toLowerCase().endsWith('</table>')) {
        i++;
        while (i < lines.length) {
          tableHtml += '\n' + lines[i];
          if (lines[i].trim().toLowerCase().endsWith('</table>')) {
            i++;
            break;
          }
          i++;
        }
      } else {
        i++;
      }
      html += renderHtmlTable(tableHtml, keywords);
      continue;
    }
    if (line.startsWith('$$')) {
      var formulaLines = [line.substring(2)];
      if (line.endsWith('$$') && line.length > 4) {
        formulaLines = [line.substring(2, line.length - 2)];
      } else {
        i++;
        while (i < lines.length && !lines[i].trim().endsWith('$$')) {
          formulaLines.push(lines[i]);
          i++;
        }
        if (i < lines.length) {
          formulaLines.push(lines[i].trim().replace(/\$\$/g, ''));
          i++;
        }
      }
      var formula = formulaLines.join('\n').trim();
      html += '<div class="block-formula">$$' + escapeHtml(formula) + '$$</div>';
      continue;
    }
    var processed = highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(line), keywords);
    processed = renderInlineFormulas(processed);
    html += '<p class="content-para">' + processed + '</p>';
    i++;
  }
  return html;
}

function transformNode(node, depth = 0, pathInFile = []) {
  const name = node.title || node.name || 'Untitled';
  const transformed = {
    name: name,
    title: node.title || node.name,
    level: node.level != null ? node.level : depth,
    depth: depth,
    summary: node.summary || '',
    keywords: node.keywords || [],
    exam_points: node.exam_points || [],
    content: node.content || '',
    mermaid: node.mermaid || '',
    tables: node.tables || [],
    captions: node.captions || [],
    _pathInFile: pathInFile,
    children: []
  };

  if (node.children && Array.isArray(node.children) && node.children.length > 0) {
    transformed.children = node.children.map((child, idx) =>
      transformNode(child, depth + 1, [...pathInFile, idx])
    );
  }

  return transformed;
}

function transformNodeWithPath(node, targetPath, depth) {
  depth = depth || 0;
  var name = node.title || node.name || 'Untitled';
  var isTarget = (depth === targetPath.length - 1 && name === targetPath[depth]);
  var isAncestor = (depth < targetPath.length - 1 && name === targetPath[depth]);
  var hasChildren = node.children && Array.isArray(node.children) && node.children.length > 0;

  var transformed = {
    name: name,
    title: node.title || node.name,
    level: node.level != null ? node.level : depth,
    depth: depth,
    summary: node.summary || '',
    keywords: node.keywords || [],
    exam_points: node.exam_points || [],
    content: node.content || '',
    mermaid: node.mermaid || '',
    tables: node.tables || [],
    captions: node.captions || [],
    children: []
  };

  if (hasChildren) {
    transformed.collapsed = !isAncestor;
    transformed.children = node.children.map(function(child) {
      return transformNodeWithPath(child, targetPath, depth + 1);
    });
  }

  if (isTarget) {
    transformed.itemStyle = {
      color: '#fbbf24',
      borderColor: '#fbbf24',
      borderWidth: 3,
      shadowBlur: 16,
      shadowColor: 'rgba(251, 191, 36, 0.5)'
    };
    transformed.label = {
      color: '#fbbf24',
      fontWeight: 'bold',
      fontSize: 13
    };
    transformed.symbolSize = 18;
  }

  return transformed;
}

async function loadAllParts() {
  const partFiles = [];
  for (let i = 1; i <= 4; i++) {
    const filename = `Part_${i}_tree_enhanced.json`;
    partFiles.push(
      fetch(`../data/tree_parts_enhanced_fixed/${filename}`)
        .then(res => {
          if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${filename}: ${res.status}`);
          return res.json();
        })
        .catch(err => {
          console.warn(`Skipping ${filename}:`, err.message);
          return null;
        })
    );
  }

  const parts = await Promise.all(partFiles);
  const validParts = parts.filter(p => p !== null);

  if (validParts.length === 0) {
    throw new Error('No data files loaded. Check that tree_parts_enhanced_fixed/ contains Part_1..4 JSON files.');
  }

  const transformedParts = validParts.map((part, idx) => {
    const node = transformNode(part, 1);
    node._sourceFile = `Part_${idx + 1}_tree_enhanced.json`;
    (function tagSource(n) {
      n._sourceFile = node._sourceFile;
      if (n.children) n.children.forEach(tagSource);
    })(node);
    if (!node.title || node.title === 'Part_' + (idx + 1)) {
      node.name = `Part ${idx + 1}`;
      node.title = `Part ${idx + 1}`;
    }
    return node;
  });

  return {
    name: 'Knowledge Tree',
    title: 'Knowledge Tree',
    level: 0,
    depth: 0,
    summary: `${validParts.length} parts loaded with enhanced data`,
    keywords: [],
    exam_points: [],
    content: '',
    children: transformedParts
  };
}

function flattenNodes(node, path, depth = 0) {
  const nodeName = node.title || node.name || 'Untitled';
  const currentPath = [...path, nodeName];
  allNodes.push({ node, path: currentPath, depth });
  if (node.children) {
    for (const child of node.children) {
      flattenNodes(child, currentPath, depth + 1);
    }
  }
}

function countNodes(node) {
  let count = 1;
  if (node.children) {
    for (const child of node.children) {
      count += countNodes(child);
    }
  }
  return count;
}

// ── Spacing Buttons ──
// ── Spacing Slider ──
var collapsedNodes = new Set();

function getNodeIndexMap(tree) {
  var map = {};
  var idx = 0;
  function walk(node) {
    var name = node.title || node.name || '';
    map[name] = idx;
    idx++;
    if (node.children) node.children.forEach(walk);
  }
  if (Array.isArray(tree)) tree.forEach(walk);
  else walk(tree);
  return map;
}

function initSpacingSlider() {
  var thumbH = document.getElementById('thumbH');
  var thumbV = document.getElementById('thumbV');
  var activeThumb = null;
  var startPos = { x: 0, y: 0 };
  var startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing };

  chart.on('expand', function(params) {
    if (params.data && (params.data.name || params.data.title))
      collapsedNodes.delete(params.data.name || params.data.title);
  });
  chart.on('collapse', function(params) {
    if (params.data && (params.data.name || params.data.title))
      collapsedNodes.add(params.data.name || params.data.title);
  });

  function valToPos(val) {
    return 10 + ((val - SPACING_MIN) / (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN)) * 110;
  }

  function updateThumbPositions() {
    thumbH.style.left = valToPos(widthSpacing) + 'px';
    thumbV.style.top = (120 - valToPos(heightSpacing)) + 'px';
  }

  function applySpacing() {
    if (!chart) return;
    var isHorizontal = currentLayout === 'LR' || currentLayout === 'RL';
    var sW = (widthSpacing - 100) / 100;
    var wFactor = 1 - sW;
    var sH = (heightSpacing - 100) / 100;
    var hFactor = 1 - sH;
    chart.setOption({
      series: [{
        top: Math.max(0.3, 4 * hFactor) + '%',
        left: Math.max(0.3, 8 * wFactor) + '%',
        right: Math.max(0.3, (isHorizontal ? 20 : 8) * wFactor) + '%',
        bottom: Math.max(0.3, 4 * hFactor) + '%'
      }]
    });
    if (collapsedNodes.size > 0) {
      var nodeMap = getNodeIndexMap(treeData);
      requestAnimationFrame(function() {
        collapsedNodes.forEach(function(name) {
          var idx = nodeMap[name];
          if (idx !== undefined) {
            chart.dispatchAction({ type: 'treeExpandAndCollapse', seriesIndex: 0, dataIndex: idx });
          }
        });
      });
    }
  }

  function getPos(e) {
    return { x: e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX,
             y: e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY };
  }

  thumbH.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'h'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; });
  thumbV.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'v'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; });
  thumbH.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'h'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; }, { passive: false });
  thumbV.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'v'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; }, { passive: false });

  document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
    if (!activeThumb) return;
    var p = getPos(e);
    if (activeThumb === 'h') {
      var dx = p.x - startPos.x;
      var newW = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.w + dx / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newW !== widthSpacing) { widthSpacing = newW; updateThumbPositions(); }
    } else {
      var dy = p.y - startPos.y;
      var newH = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.h - dy / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newH !== heightSpacing) { heightSpacing = newH; updateThumbPositions(); }
    }
  });

  document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
    if (activeThumb) { applySpacing(); activeThumb = null; }
  });

  document.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
    if (!activeThumb) return;
    var p = getPos(e);
    if (activeThumb === 'h') {
      var dx = p.x - startPos.x;
      var newW = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.w + dx / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newW !== widthSpacing) { widthSpacing = newW; updateThumbPositions(); }
    } else {
      var dy = p.y - startPos.y;
      var newH = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.h - dy / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newH !== heightSpacing) { heightSpacing = newH; updateThumbPositions(); }
    }
  }, { passive: false });

  document.addEventListener('touchend', function() {
    if (activeThumb) { applySpacing(); activeThumb = null; }
  });

  updateThumbPositions();
}

async function initChart() {
  const chartContainer = document.getElementById('chart');
  chart = echarts.init(chartContainer, null, { renderer: 'canvas', devicePixelRatio: window.devicePixelRatio * 2 });

  try {
    treeData = await loadAllParts();
    allNodes = [];
    flattenNodes(treeData, []);

    const totalNodes = allNodes.length;
    const partCount = (treeData.children || []).length;
    const enhancedCount = allNodes.filter(n => n.node.summary && n.node.summary.length > 0).length;
    document.getElementById('stats').textContent =
      `Nodes: ${totalNodes} | Parts: ${partCount} | Enhanced: ${enhancedCount}`;

    document.getElementById('searchToggleBtn').style.display = 'flex';
    renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
    initSpacingSlider();

    document.getElementById('layoutSelect').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
      currentLayout = e.target.value;
      renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
    });

    document.getElementById('expandLevel').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
      currentExpandLevel = parseInt(e.target.value);
      renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
    });

    chart.on('click', (params) => {
      if (editState.active) {
        if (params.componentSubType === 'tree' && params.data !== editState.nodeData) {
          saveEdit(editState.inputEl.value);
        }
        return;
      }
      if (params.componentSubType === 'tree') {
        showNodeInfo(params.data);
      }
    });

    chart.on('dblclick', (params) => {
      if (params.componentSubType === 'tree') {
        startEdit(params.data, params.event);
      }
    });

    document.getElementById('chartContainer').addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
      if (!editState.active) return;
      if (e.target === document.getElementById('inlineEditor')) return;
      saveEdit(editState.inputEl.value);
    });

    document.getElementById('inlineEditor').addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (!editState.active) return;
      if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        e.preventDefault();
        saveEdit(this.value);
      } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        e.preventDefault();
        cancelEdit();
      }
    });

    window.addEventListener('resize', () => chart.resize());

  } catch (error) {
    chartContainer.innerHTML = `<div style="color: #ef4444; padding: 24px; font-size: 14px;">
      <strong>Error loading data</strong><br/>${error.message}<br/><br/>
      <span style="color: #71717a;">Make sure you are serving this file via HTTP (e.g. <code>python -m http.server</code>), not opening directly as file://</span>
    </div>`;
  }
}

function getLabelPosition(layout) {
  if (layout === 'LR') return 'right';
  if (layout === 'RL') return 'left';
  if (layout === 'TB') return 'bottom';
  return 'top';
}

function getLeafLabelPosition(layout) {
  if (layout === 'LR') return 'right';
  if (layout === 'RL') return 'left';
  if (layout === 'TB') return 'bottom';
  return 'top';
}

function renderChart(layout, expandLevel, targetPath) {
  const isHorizontal = layout === 'LR' || layout === 'RL';
  var ws = (widthSpacing - 100) / 20;
  var wFactor = 1 - ws * 0.7;
  var leftMargin = Math.max(0.5, 8 * wFactor);
  var rightMargin = Math.max(0.5, (isHorizontal ? 20 : 8) * wFactor);
  var hs = (heightSpacing - 100) / 20;
  var hFactor = 1 - hs * 0.7;
  var topMargin = Math.max(0.5, 4 * hFactor);
  var bottomMargin = Math.max(0.5, 4 * hFactor);

  var data;
  if (targetPath && targetPath.length > 0) {
    data = [transformNodeWithPath(treeData, targetPath)];
  } else {
    data = [treeData];
  }

  const option = {
    backgroundColor: 'transparent',
    tooltip: {
      trigger: 'item',
      triggerOn: 'mousemove',
      confine: false,
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      borderColor: 'transparent',
      borderWidth: 0,
      padding: 0,
      textStyle: { color: '#e4e4e7', fontSize: 12, lineHeight: 20 },
      extraCssText: 'white-space: normal; word-wrap: break-word; overflow-wrap: break-word;',
      formatter: function(params) {
        if (params.componentSubType !== 'tree') return '';
        const d = params.data;
        const c = getTooltipColors();
        let html = `<div style="max-width:480px;word-wrap:break-word;overflow-wrap:break-word;background:${c.bg};border:1px solid ${c.divider};border-radius:8px;padding:16px 20px;">`;
        html += `<div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:${c.title};margin-bottom:6px;">${d.name}</div>`;

        if (d.level != null) {
          html += `<span style="font-size:10px;color:${c.meta};">Level ${d.level}</span>`;
        }

        if (d.summary) {
          html += `<div class="tooltip-summary" style="margin-top:8px;">${formatSummary(d.summary, d.keywords, 0)}</div>`;
        }

        if (d.keywords && d.keywords.length > 0) {
          html += `<div style="margin-top:8px;">`;
          html += d.keywords.map(k =>
            `<span style="display:inline-block;background:${c.keywordBg};color:${c.keywordColor};padding:1px 6px;border-radius:3px;font-size:10px;margin:1px 2px;">${k}</span>`
          ).join('');
          html += `</div>`;
        }

        if (d.exam_points && d.exam_points.length > 0) {
          html += `<div style="margin-top:8px;border-top:1px solid ${c.divider};padding-top:6px;">`;
          d.exam_points.forEach(ep => {
            const freqColor = ep.frequency === '高频' ? '#22c55e' : ep.frequency === '中频' ? '#eab308' : '#71717a';
            html += `<div style="font-size:11px;margin:3px 0;"><span style="color:${freqColor};">${ep.frequency || ''}</span> <span style="color:${c.meta};">[${ep.type || ''}]</span> ${ep.point}</div>`;
          });
          html += `</div>`;
        }

        if (d.captions && d.captions.length > 0) {
          html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;border-top:1px solid ${c.divider};padding-top:6px;">`;
          html += `<div style="font-size:10px;color:${c.meta};margin-bottom:4px;">CHARTS &amp; TABLES</div>`;
          d.captions.forEach(cap => {
            html += `<div style="font-size:11px;margin:2px 0;color:${c.body};"><b>${cap.label}</b>: ${cap.text}</div>`;
          });
          html += `</div>`;
        }

        if (d.content) {
          html += `<div class="tooltip-content" style="margin-top:6px;border-top:1px solid ${c.divider};padding-top:6px;">${formatContent(d.content, d.keywords, 0)}</div>`;
        }

        if (d.mermaid) {
          html += `<div style="margin-top:4px;font-size:10px;color:${c.meta};">[Flowchart - click for details]</div>`;
        }
        if (d.tables && d.tables.length > 0) {
          html += `<div style="margin-top:4px;font-size:10px;color:${c.meta};">[${d.tables.length} table(s) - click for details]</div>`;
        }

        if (d.children && d.children.length > 0) {
          html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;font-size:10px;color:${c.meta};">${d.children.length} child nodes</div>`;
        }

        html += `</div>`;
        return html;
      }
    },
    series: [
      {
        type: 'tree',
        data: data,
        top: topMargin + '%',
        left: leftMargin + '%',
        right: rightMargin + '%',
        bottom: bottomMargin + '%',
        orient: layout,
        symbol: 'circle',
        symbolSize: function(value, params) {
          const d = params.data;
          if (d.symbolSize) return d.symbolSize;
          const level = d.level || 0;
          if (level === 0) return [20, 20];
          if (level === 1) return [14, 14];
          if (level === 2) return [10, 10];
          return [7, 7];
        },
        initialTreeDepth: (targetPath && targetPath.length > 0) ? -1 : expandLevel,
        expandAndCollapse: true,
        animationDuration: 500,
        animationDurationUpdate: 500,
        animationEasing: 'cubicOut',
        roam: true,
        itemStyle: {
          borderWidth: 1.5,
          borderColor: function(params) {
            if (params.data.itemStyle && params.data.itemStyle.borderColor) {
              return params.data.itemStyle.borderColor;
            }
            return getNodeColor(params.data.level || 0) + '80';
          },
          color: function(params) {
            if (params.data.itemStyle && params.data.itemStyle.color) {
              return params.data.itemStyle.color;
            }
            return getNodeColor(params.data.level || 0);
          }
        },
        label: {
          position: getLabelPosition(layout),
          verticalAlign: 'middle',
          align: 'left',
          fontSize: 12,
          color: getChartLabelColor(),
          fontWeight: 500,
          formatter: function(params) {
            const d = params.data;
            const name = d.name || '';
            if (d.summary && d.summary.length > 0 && d.level > 0) {
              return `{enhanced|} ${name}`;
            }
            return name;
          },
          rich: {
            enhanced: {
              backgroundColor: 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.3)',
              borderRadius: 3,
              width: 4,
              height: 4
            }
          }
        },
        leaves: {
          label: {
            position: getLeafLabelPosition(layout),
            verticalAlign: 'middle',
            align: 'left',
            fontSize: 11,
            color: getChartLeafLabelColor()
          }
        },
        lineStyle: {
          color: 'rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.2)',
          width: 1.5,
          curveness: 0.5
        },
        emphasis: {
          itemStyle: {
            color: '#fbbf24',
            borderColor: '#fbbf24',
            borderWidth: 2,
            shadowBlur: 12,
            shadowColor: 'rgba(251, 191, 36, 0.3)'
          },
          label: {
            color: '#fbbf24',
            fontWeight: 'bold',
            fontSize: 13
          }
        },
        edgeShape: 'curve'
      }
    ]
  };

  chart.setOption(option, true);
}

function showNodeInfo(d) {
  const panel = document.getElementById('infoPanel');
  const content = document.getElementById('infoContent');
  currentDisplayNode = d;
  let html = `<div class="node-title">${d.name}</div>`;

  if (d.level != null) {
    html += `<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);">Level ${d.level}</span>`;
  }

  if (d.summary) {
    html += `<div class="field-label">Summary</div>`;
    html += `<div class="summary">${formatSummary(d.summary, d.keywords, 0)}</div>`;
  }

  if (d.keywords && d.keywords.length > 0) {
    html += `<div class="field-label">Keywords</div>`;
    html += `<div class="keywords">`;
    html += d.keywords.map(k => `<span class="keyword-tag">${k}</span>`).join('');
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if (d.exam_points && d.exam_points.length > 0) {
    html += `<div class="field-label">Exam Points</div>`;
    d.exam_points.forEach(ep => {
      const freqColor = ep.frequency === '高频' ? 'var(--green)' :
                         ep.frequency === '中频' ? 'var(--yellow)' : 'var(--text3)';
      html += `<div class="exam-point">
        ${ep.point}
        <div class="exam-meta">
          <span style="color:${freqColor};">${ep.frequency || '-'}</span> &middot; ${ep.type || '-'}
        </div>
      </div>`;
    });
  }

  if (d.captions && d.captions.length > 0) {
    html += `<div class="field-label">Charts &amp; Tables</div>`;
    d.captions.forEach(cap => {
      html += `<div class="caption-item"><b>${cap.label}</b>: ${cap.text}</div>`;
    });
  }

  if (d.content && d.content.length > 0) {
    html += `<div class="field-label">Content <button class="content-edit-btn" id="contentEditBtn" onclick="enterContentEdit()">Edit</button></div>`;
    html += `<div class="content-display" id="contentDisplay">${formatContent(d.content, d.keywords, 0)}</div>`;
    html += `<div class="content-editor-wrap" id="contentEditorWrap">`;
    html += `  <div class="content-edit-bar">`;
    html += `    <button id="fmtBold" onclick="execFmt('bold')" title="Bold (Ctrl+B)"><b>B</b></button>`;
    html += `    <button id="fmtItalic" onclick="execFmt('italic')" title="Italic (Ctrl+I)"><i>I</i></button>`;
    html += `    <button id="fmtStrike" onclick="execFmt('strikethrough')" title="Strikethrough"><s>S</s></button>`;
    html += `  </div>`;
    html += `  <div class="content-editable" id="contentEditable" contenteditable="true"></div>`;
    html += `  <div class="content-actions">`;
    html += `    <button class="btn-save" onclick="saveContentEdit()">Save</button>`;
    html += `    <button class="btn-cancel" onclick="cancelContentEdit()">Cancel</button>`;
    html += `  </div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
  }

  if (d.mermaid) {
    html += renderNodeMermaid(d.mermaid, 'info-mermaid-' + Date.now());
  }

  if (d.tables && d.tables.length > 0) {
    html += renderNodeTables(d.tables);
  }

  if (d.children && d.children.length > 0) {
    html += `<div style="margin-top:10px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);">${d.children.length} child node(s)</div>`;
  }

  content.innerHTML = html;
  panel.classList.add('show');
  postRenderMathAndMermaid(content);
}

function closePanel() {
  document.getElementById('infoPanel').classList.remove('show');
  currentDisplayNode = null;
}

// ── Content Editor ──

function enterContentEdit() {
  if (!currentDisplayNode) return;
  const display = document.getElementById('contentDisplay');
  const editorWrap = document.getElementById('contentEditorWrap');
  const editable = document.getElementById('contentEditable');
  const btn = document.getElementById('contentEditBtn');

  const raw = currentDisplayNode.content || '';
  editable.innerHTML = raw.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/\n/g, '<br>');

  display.classList.add('hidden');
  editorWrap.classList.add('active');
  btn.style.display = 'none';
  editable.focus();
}

function cancelContentEdit() {
  const display = document.getElementById('contentDisplay');
  const editorWrap = document.getElementById('contentEditorWrap');
  const btn = document.getElementById('contentEditBtn');

  editorWrap.classList.remove('active');
  display.classList.remove('hidden');
  btn.style.display = '';
}

async function saveContentEdit() {
  if (!currentDisplayNode) return;
  const editable = document.getElementById('contentEditable');
  const newText = editable.innerText.trim();

  currentDisplayNode.content = newText;

  const sourceFile = currentDisplayNode._sourceFile || '';
  if (sourceFile) {
    try {
      const resp = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/update-node`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          filename: sourceFile,
          path: currentDisplayNode._pathInFile || [],
          title: currentDisplayNode.name || currentDisplayNode.title,
          content: newText
        })
      });
      if (!resp.ok) {
        const err = await resp.json();
        console.warn('Content save failed:', err.error || resp.status);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('Content save failed:', e.message);
    }
  }

  const display = document.getElementById('contentDisplay');
  display.innerHTML = formatContent(newText, currentDisplayNode.keywords || [], 0);
  postRenderMathAndMermaid(display);
  cancelContentEdit();
}

function execFmt(command) {
  document.execCommand(command, false, null);
  document.getElementById('contentEditable').focus();
}

function fitView() {
  if (!chart) return;
  chart.setOption({}, { replaceMerge: ['series'] });
  renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
}

function expandAll() {
  if (!chart) return;
  currentExpandLevel = 5;
  document.getElementById('expandLevel').value = '5';
  renderChart(currentLayout, 5);
}

function collapseAll() {
  if (!chart) return;
  currentExpandLevel = 1;
  document.getElementById('expandLevel').value = '1';
  renderChart(currentLayout, 1);
}

// ── Inline Node Editing ──

function getSourceFile(nodeData) {
  return nodeData._sourceFile || '';
}

function startEdit(nodeData, event) {
  if (editState.active) {
    saveEdit(editState.inputEl.value);
  }

  const input = document.getElementById('inlineEditor');
  const hint = document.getElementById('editHint');

  const container = document.getElementById('chartContainer');
  const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
  const left = event.clientX - rect.left - 90;
  const top = event.clientY - rect.top - 14;
  input.style.left = Math.max(4, left) + 'px';
  input.style.top = Math.max(4, top) + 'px';
  input.value = nodeData.name || '';
  input.classList.add('active');
  hint.classList.add('active');

  input.focus();
  input.select();

  editState.active = true;
  editState.nodeData = nodeData;
  editState.inputEl = input;
}

async function saveEdit(newTitle) {
  if (!editState.active) return;

  newTitle = (newTitle || '').trim();
  const nodeData = editState.nodeData;

  if (!newTitle || newTitle === nodeData.name) {
    cleanupEdit();
    return;
  }

  nodeData.name = newTitle;
  nodeData.title = newTitle;

  const sourceFile = getSourceFile(nodeData);
  if (sourceFile) {
    try {
      const resp = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/update-node`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          filename: sourceFile,
          path: nodeData._pathInFile || [],
          title: newTitle
        })
      });
      if (!resp.ok) {
        const err = await resp.json();
        console.warn('Save to server failed:', err.error || resp.status);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('Save to server failed:', e.message);
    }
  }

  cleanupEdit();
  renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
}

function cancelEdit() {
  if (!editState.active) return;
  cleanupEdit();
}

function cleanupEdit() {
  const input = document.getElementById('inlineEditor');
  const hint = document.getElementById('editHint');
  input.classList.remove('active');
  hint.classList.remove('active');
  editState.active = false;
  editState.nodeData = null;
  editState.inputEl = null;
}

// ── Search ──

function toggleSearch() {
  searchExpanded = !searchExpanded;
  var panel = document.getElementById('searchPanel');
  var toggleBtn = document.getElementById('searchToggleBtn');

  if (searchExpanded) {
    panel.classList.remove('collapsed');
    toggleBtn.classList.add('shifted');
    document.getElementById('searchInput').focus();
  } else {
    panel.classList.add('collapsed');
    toggleBtn.classList.remove('shifted');
  }
}

function performSearch() {
  var input = document.getElementById('searchInput');
  var query = input.value.trim();
  var clearBtn = document.getElementById('searchClearBtn');
  var resultsEl = document.getElementById('searchResults');
  var statusEl = document.getElementById('searchStatus');

  if (!query) {
    clearBtn.style.display = 'none';
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">Type to search node titles...</div>';
    statusEl.textContent = '';
    return;
  }

  clearBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';

  if (!allNodes || allNodes.length === 0) {
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">No tree data loaded</div>';
    statusEl.textContent = '';
    return;
  }

  var queryLower = query.toLowerCase();
  var matches = [];

  for (var i = 0; i < allNodes.length; i++) {
    var nodeData = allNodes[i];
    var title = (nodeData.node.title || nodeData.node.name || '').toLowerCase();
    if (title.indexOf(queryLower) !== -1) {
      matches.push({ index: i, node: nodeData.node, path: nodeData.path });
    }
  }

  if (matches.length === 0) {
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">No matching nodes found</div>';
    statusEl.textContent = '';
    return;
  }

  statusEl.textContent = matches.length + ' node(s) found';

  var html = '';
  for (var m = 0; m < matches.length; m++) {
    var match = matches[m];
    var pathHtml = '';
    for (var p = 0; p < match.path.length; p++) {
      if (p > 0) pathHtml += '<span class="path-sep">&#9654;</span>';
      pathHtml += escapeHtml(match.path[p] || '');
    }

    var title = match.node.title || match.node.name || '';
    var titleLower = title.toLowerCase();
    var queryLen = query.length;
    var titleHtml = '';
    var lastIdx = 0;
    var idx = titleLower.indexOf(queryLower);
    while (idx !== -1) {
      titleHtml += escapeHtml(title.substring(lastIdx, idx));
      titleHtml += '<span class="search-highlight">' + escapeHtml(title.substring(idx, idx + queryLen)) + '</span>';
      lastIdx = idx + queryLen;
      idx = titleLower.indexOf(queryLower, lastIdx);
    }
    titleHtml += escapeHtml(title.substring(lastIdx));

    html += '<div class="search-result-item" data-node-index="' + match.index + '" onclick="expandToNode(' + match.index + ')">';
    html += '<div class="search-result-path">' + pathHtml + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="search-result-title">' + titleHtml + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
  }

  resultsEl.innerHTML = html;
}

function expandToNode(nodeIndex) {
  if (!chart || !treeData || nodeIndex >= allNodes.length) return;

  var targetPath = allNodes[nodeIndex].path;

  var items = document.querySelectorAll('.search-result-item');
  for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
    items[i].classList.remove('active');
  }
  var activeItem = document.querySelector('.search-result-item[data-node-index="' + nodeIndex + '"]');
  if (activeItem) activeItem.classList.add('active');

  renderChart(currentLayout, -1, targetPath);
}

function clearSearch() {
  document.getElementById('searchInput').value = '';
  document.getElementById('searchClearBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('searchResults').innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">Type to search node titles...</div>';
  document.getElementById('searchStatus').textContent = '';
  if (chart && treeData) {
    renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
  }
}

document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
  if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'f') {
    if (treeData) {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (!searchExpanded) toggleSearch();
      document.getElementById('searchInput').focus();
      document.getElementById('searchInput').select();
    }
  }
  if (e.key === 'Escape' && searchExpanded) {
    toggleSearch();
  }
});

// ── Zoom Slider ──
let currentZoom = 1;
function updateZoom(zoom) {
  currentZoom = zoom;
  const container = document.getElementById('chartContainer');
  container.style.transform = `scale(${zoom})`;
  container.style.transformOrigin = 'center center';
  container.style.transition = 'transform 0.15s ease';
  document.getElementById('zoomLabel').textContent = Math.round(zoom * 100) + '%';
  document.getElementById('zoomRange').value = Math.round(zoom * 100);
}
document.getElementById('zoomRange').addEventListener('input', function(e) {
  updateZoom(parseInt(e.target.value) / 100);
});

window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initChart);
</script>
</body>
</html>

<div class="spacing-slider" id="spacingSlider" title="Drag to adjust node spacing">
  <div class="spacing-label">SPACING</div>
  <div class="cross-area" id="crossArea">
    <div class="track-h"></div>

    <div class="thumb thumb-v" id="thumbV"></div>
