</div>

<script>
const API_BASE = window.location.origin || 'http://localhost:8700';

// ── Theme ──
(function() {
  var saved = localStorage.getItem('kt-theme');
  if (saved === 'light') document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
  updateThemeUI();
  // Show config overlay first on page load
  loadSavedConfig();
  document.getElementById('configOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
  document.getElementById('uploadOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
})();
function toggleTheme() {
  var html = document.documentElement;
  var isLight = html.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light';
  if (isLight) { html.removeAttribute('data-theme'); localStorage.setItem('kt-theme', 'dark'); }
  else { html.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light'); localStorage.setItem('kt-theme', 'light'); }
  updateThemeUI();
  mermaid.initialize({
    startOnLoad: false,
    theme: document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? 'default' : 'dark',
    securityLevel: 'loose',
    fontFamily: '-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Segoe UI, sans-serif'
  });
  if (chart && treeData) renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
}
function updateThemeUI() {
  var isLight = document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light';
  document.getElementById('themeIcon').textContent = isLight ? '☀️' : '🌙';
  document.getElementById('themeLabel').textContent = isLight ? 'Light' : 'Dark';
}
function getTooltipColors() {
  var isLight = document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light';
  return isLight
    ? { bg: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.98)', text: '#1a1a2e', meta: '#6b7280', title: '#4f46e5', body: '#4a4a6a', divider: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.12)', keywordBg: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.08)', keywordColor: '#4f46e5' }
    : { bg: 'rgba(15,17,23,0.96)', text: '#e4e4e7', meta: '#71717a', title: '#818cf8', body: '#a1a1aa', divider: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.15)', keywordBg: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.12)', keywordColor: '#818cf8' };
}
function getChartLabelColor() {
  return document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? '#1a1a2e' : '#e4e4e7';
}
function getChartLeafLabelColor() {
  return document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? '#6b7280' : '#a1a1aa';
}

// ── Mermaid Init ──
mermaid.initialize({
  startOnLoad: false,
  theme: document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light' ? 'default' : 'dark',
  securityLevel: 'loose',
  fontFamily: '-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Segoe UI, sans-serif'
});

let chart = null;
let treeData = null;
let allNodes = [];
let currentLayout = 'LR';
let currentExpandLevel = 2;
let widthSpacing = 100;
let heightSpacing = 100;
const SPACING_MIN = 20;
const SPACING_MAX = 300;
let selectedFiles = [];
let currentTaskId = null;
let currentDisplayNode = null;
let searchExpanded = false;

const STAGE_LABELS = {
  splitting: 'Preparing documents...',
  ocr_converting: 'Extracting text...',
  building_tree: 'Building knowledge tree...',
  ai_enhancing: 'AI enhancement in progress...',
  merging: 'Preparing final data...',
  complete: 'Processing complete!'
};

const LEVEL_COLORS = [
  '#6366f1', '#818cf8', '#22c55e', '#eab308', '#f97316', '#a78bfa'
];

function getNodeColor(level) {
  return LEVEL_COLORS[Math.min(level, LEVEL_COLORS.length - 1)];
}

// ── API Config ──

const CONFIG_STORAGE_KEY = 'kt-api-config';

function loadSavedConfig() {
  try {
    var raw = localStorage.getItem(CONFIG_STORAGE_KEY);
    if (raw) {
      var cfg = JSON.parse(raw);
      if (cfg.mineruToken) document.getElementById('mineruToken').value = cfg.mineruToken;
      if (cfg.deepseekKey) document.getElementById('deepseekKey').value = cfg.deepseekKey;
    }
  } catch (e) {}
}

function saveConfigToStorage() {
  var cfg = {
    mineruToken: document.getElementById('mineruToken').value.trim(),
    deepseekKey: document.getElementById('deepseekKey').value.trim()
  };
  if (cfg.mineruToken || cfg.deepseekKey) {
    localStorage.setItem(CONFIG_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(cfg));
  }
}

function getConfig() {
  try {
    var raw = localStorage.getItem(CONFIG_STORAGE_KEY);
    if (raw) return JSON.parse(raw);
  } catch (e) {}
  return {};
}

function saveConfigAndContinue() {
  saveConfigToStorage();
  document.getElementById('configOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('uploadOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function skipConfig() {
  document.getElementById('configOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('uploadOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
}

function showConfigFromUpload() {
  loadSavedConfig();
  document.getElementById('uploadOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('configOverlay').classList.remove('hidden');
}

// ── File Upload ──

const uploadOverlay = document.getElementById('uploadOverlay');
const uploadBox = document.getElementById('uploadBox');
const fileInput = document.getElementById('fileInput');
const selectedFileEl = document.getElementById('selectedFile');
const fileNameEl = document.getElementById('fileName');
const fileSizeEl = document.getElementById('fileSize');
const startBtn = document.getElementById('startBtn');
const folderInput = document.getElementById('folderInput');

const ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS = ['.pdf', '.docx', '.txt'];
function isAcceptedFile(file) {
  if (file.type === 'application/pdf') return true;
  if (file.type === 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document') return true;
  if (file.type === 'text/plain') return true;
  const ext = '.' + file.name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
  return ACCEPTED_EXTENSIONS.includes(ext);
}

fileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
  const files = Array.from(e.target.files).filter(isAcceptedFile);
  setSelectedFiles(files);
});

function formatSize(bytes) {
  if (bytes < 1024) return bytes + ' B';
  if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return (bytes / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB';
  return (bytes / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' MB';
}

function setSelectedFiles(files) {
  selectedFiles = files;
  if (!selectedFiles.length) {
    selectedFileEl.style.display = 'none';
    startBtn.style.display = 'none';
    return;
  }

  const totalBytes = selectedFiles.reduce((sum, file) => sum + file.size, 0);
  const previewNames = selectedFiles.slice(0, 3).map(file => file.name).join(' | ');
  const moreText = selectedFiles.length > 3 ? ` | +${selectedFiles.length - 3} more` : '';
  fileNameEl.textContent = selectedFiles.length === 1 ? selectedFiles[0].name : `${selectedFiles.length} PDFs selected`;
  fileSizeEl.textContent = `${formatSize(totalBytes)} | ${previewNames}${moreText}`;
  selectedFileEl.style.display = 'flex';
  startBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';
}

// Drag and drop
uploadBox.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
  e.preventDefault();
  uploadBox.classList.add('drag-over');
});
uploadBox.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
  uploadBox.classList.remove('drag-over');
});
uploadBox.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
  e.preventDefault();
  uploadBox.classList.remove('drag-over');
  const files = Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files).filter(isAcceptedFile);
  if (files.length > 0) {
    setSelectedFiles(files);
  } else {
    showToast('Please upload a PDF, Word, or TXT file');
  }
});

// ── Open Existing Project ──

folderInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
  const files = Array.from(e.target.files);
  if (!files.length) return;
  openExistingProject(files);
});

function findTreeJson(files) {
  for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
    var f = files[i];
    var rel = f.webkitRelativePath || f.name;
    if (rel.endsWith('json/knowledge_tree.json') || rel.endsWith('json\\knowledge_tree.json')) return f;
  }
  for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
    var f = files[i];
    var rel = f.webkitRelativePath || f.name;
    if (rel.endsWith('knowledge_tree.json')) return f;
  }
  return null;
}

function openExistingProject(files) {
  var treeFile = findTreeJson(files);
  if (!treeFile) {
    var names = files.slice(0, 8).map(function(f) { return f.webkitRelativePath || f.name; }).join('\n');
    showToast('No json/knowledge_tree.json found in selected folder. Files found:\n' + names);
    folderInput.value = '';
    return;
  }

  var reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = function() {
    try {
      var data = JSON.parse(reader.result);
      uploadOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
      enterPreview(data);
      showToast('Project loaded successfully!');
    } catch (err) {
      showToast('Failed to parse knowledge_tree.json: ' + err.message);
    }
  };
  reader.onerror = function() {
    showToast('Failed to read json/knowledge_tree.json');
  };
  reader.readAsText(treeFile);
  folderInput.value = '';
}

// ── Processing ──

async function startProcessing() {
  if (!selectedFiles.length) return;

  uploadOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
  const progressOverlay = document.getElementById('progressOverlay');
  progressOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');

  resetStages();
  updateProgress(0, 'splitting', `Uploading ${selectedFiles.length} file(s)...`);

  try {
    const formData = new FormData();
    selectedFiles.forEach(file => formData.append('files', file));

    // Attach API configuration
    var config = getConfig();
    if (config.mineruToken) formData.append('mineru_token', config.mineruToken);
    if (config.deepseekKey) formData.append('deepseek_api_key', config.deepseekKey);

    const uploadRes = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/upload`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData
    });

    if (!uploadRes.ok) {
      throw new Error(`Upload failed: ${uploadRes.status}`);
    }

    const { task_id } = await uploadRes.json();
    currentTaskId = task_id;
    await pollTask(task_id);

  } catch (err) {
    updateProgress(0, '', `Error: ${err.message}`);
    showToast(`Processing failed: ${err.message}`);
    setTimeout(() => {
      progressOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
      uploadOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');
    }, 2000);
  }
}

async function pollTask(taskId) {
  while (true) {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/status/${taskId}`);
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Status check failed: ${res.status}`);

      const data = await res.json();

      if (data.status === 'error') {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Unknown error');
      }

      updateProgress(data.progress, data.stage, data.messages?.[data.messages.length - 1] || '');

      if (data.status === 'done') {
        await loadResult(taskId);
        return;
      }
    } catch (err) {
      throw err;
    }
    await sleep(800);
  }
}

async function loadResult(taskId) {
  const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/result/${taskId}`);
  if (!res.ok) {
    throw new Error(`Failed to load result: ${res.status}`);
  }

  const data = await res.json();
  enterPreview(data);
}

function enterPreview(data) {
  treeData = data;
  allNodes = [];
  flattenNodes(treeData, []);

  const totalNodes = allNodes.length;
  const parts = (treeData.children || []).length;
  const enhanced = allNodes.filter(n => n.node.summary && n.node.summary.length > 0).length;
  document.getElementById('stats').textContent = `Nodes: ${totalNodes} | PDFs: ${parts} | Enhanced: ${enhanced}`;

  document.getElementById('progressOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('headerControls').style.display = 'flex';
  document.getElementById('exportBtn').style.display = 'inline-block';
  document.getElementById('chart').classList.remove('loading-placeholder');
  document.getElementById('chart').innerHTML = '';
  document.getElementById('searchToggleBtn').style.display = 'flex';

  initChart();
  renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
}

function resetAndUpload() {
  treeData = null;
  allNodes = [];
  selectedFiles = [];
  currentTaskId = null;
  if (chart) {
    chart.dispose();
    chart = null;
  }

  if (searchExpanded) toggleSearch();
  document.getElementById('searchToggleBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('headerControls').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('exportBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('chart').classList.add('loading-placeholder');
  document.getElementById('chart').innerHTML = '<span class="big-icon">📂</span><span>Upload one or more PDFs to generate the Knowledge Tree Mind Map</span>';
  document.getElementById('stats').textContent = '';
  document.getElementById('infoPanel').classList.remove('show');

  fileInput.value = '';
  folderInput.value = '';
  selectedFileEl.style.display = 'none';
  startBtn.style.display = 'none';
  uploadOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');
}

function updateProgress(progress, stage, message) {
  document.getElementById('progressBar').style.width = progress + '%';
  document.getElementById('progressMessage').innerHTML =
    `<span class="spinner-small"></span>${message || STAGE_LABELS[stage] || ''} (${Math.round(progress)}%)`;

  resetStages();
  const stageMap = {
    splitting: 'stage-splitting',
    ocr_converting: 'stage-ocr_converting',
    building_tree: 'stage-building_tree',
    ai_enhancing: 'stage-ai_enhancing',
  };

  let foundActive = false;
  for (const [key, elId] of Object.entries(stageMap)) {
    const el = document.getElementById(elId);
    if (!foundActive && key === stage && progress < 90) {
      el.classList.add('active');
      foundActive = true;
    } else if (!foundActive) {
      el.classList.add('done');
    }
  }

  if (progress >= 90) {
    document.getElementById('stage-complete').classList.add('done');
  }
}

function resetStages() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.progress-stage').forEach(el => {
    el.classList.remove('active', 'done');
  });
}

// ── Mind Map Rendering (from tree_mindmap.html) ──

function formatSummary(summary, keywords, maxLen) {
  if (!summary) return '';
  var text = summary;
  if (maxLen > 0 && text.length > maxLen) {
    text = text.substring(0, maxLen) + '…';
  }
  var sentences = text.split(/(?<=[。；])/);
  var groupSize = 3;
  var html = '';
  for (var i = 0; i < sentences.length; i += groupSize) {
    var chunk = sentences.slice(i, i + groupSize).join('');
    if (keywords && keywords.length > 0) {
      keywords.forEach(function(kw) {
        if (kw.length >= 2) {
          var escaped = kw.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
          var regex = new RegExp('(' + escaped + ')', 'g');
          chunk = chunk.replace(regex, '<span class="sum-hl">$1</span>');
        }
      });
    }
    html += '<p class="sum-para">' + chunk + '</p>';
  }
  return html;
}

function escapeHtml(text) {
  return text.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
}

function highlightKeywords(text, keywords) {
  if (!keywords || keywords.length === 0) return text;
  var result = text;
  keywords.forEach(function(kw) {
    if (kw.length >= 2) {
      var escaped = kw.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
      var regex = new RegExp('(' + escaped + ')', 'g');
      result = result.replace(regex, '<span class="sum-hl">$1</span>');
    }
  });
  return result;
}

function renderInlineFormulas(text) {
  text = text.replace(/\$\$(.+?)\$\$/g, '<span class="inline-formula" data-formula="$$$1$$">$$$1$$</span>');
  text = text.replace(/(?<!\$)\$(?!\$)(.+?)(?<!\$)\$(?!\$)/g,
    '<span class="inline-formula" data-formula="$$$1$">$$$1$</span>');
  return text;
}

function renderMarkdownTable(tableLines, keywords) {
  if (tableLines.length < 2) return '';
  var headerCells = tableLines[0].split('|').filter(function(c) { return c.trim() !== ''; });
  var dataStart = 1;
  if (tableLines.length > 1 && /^[\s|:-]+$/.test(tableLines[1])) {
    dataStart = 2;
  }
  var html = '<div class="table-wrapper"><table class="md-table"><thead><tr>';
  headerCells.forEach(function(cell) {
    html += '<th>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.trim()), keywords) + '</th>';
  });
  html += '</tr></thead><tbody>';
  for (var r = dataStart; r < tableLines.length; r++) {
    var cells = tableLines[r].split('|').filter(function(c) { return c.trim() !== ''; });
    html += '<tr>';
    cells.forEach(function(cell) {
      html += '<td>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.trim()), keywords) + '</td>';
    });
    html += '</tr>';
  }
  html += '</tbody></table></div>';
  return html;
}

function renderHtmlTable(htmlString, keywords) {
  try {
    var parser = new DOMParser();
    var doc = parser.parseFromString(htmlString, 'text/html');
    var table = doc.querySelector('table');
    if (!table) return escapeHtml(htmlString);
    var rows = table.querySelectorAll('tr');
    if (rows.length === 0) return '';
    var html = '<div class="table-wrapper"><table class="md-table">';
    var firstRowCells = rows[0].querySelectorAll('td, th');
    var hasHead = table.querySelector('thead') || (firstRowCells.length > 0 && firstRowCells[0].tagName === 'TH');
    var startRow = 0;
    if (hasHead) {
      html += '<thead><tr>';
      firstRowCells.forEach(function(cell) {
        var colspan = cell.getAttribute('colspan') || 1;
        var rowspan = cell.getAttribute('rowspan') || 1;
        html += '<th' + (colspan > 1 ? ' colspan="' + colspan + '"' : '')
             + (rowspan > 1 ? ' rowspan="' + rowspan + '"' : '')
             + '>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.textContent.trim()), keywords) + '</th>';
      });
      html += '</tr></thead><tbody>';
      startRow = 1;
    } else {
      html += '<tbody>';
    }
    for (var r = startRow; r < rows.length; r++) {
      html += '<tr>';
      var cells = rows[r].querySelectorAll('td, th');
      cells.forEach(function(cell) {
        var colspan = cell.getAttribute('colspan') || 1;
        var rowspan = cell.getAttribute('rowspan') || 1;
        html += '<td' + (colspan > 1 ? ' colspan="' + colspan + '"' : '')
             + (rowspan > 1 ? ' rowspan="' + rowspan + '"' : '')
             + '>' + highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(cell.textContent.trim()), keywords) + '</td>';
      });
      html += '</tr>';
    }
    html += '</tbody></table></div>';
    return html;
  } catch(e) {
    return escapeHtml(htmlString);
  }
}

function renderNodeMermaid(mermaidCode, containerId) {
  if (!mermaidCode) return '';
  return '<div class="field-label">Flowchart</div>'
    + '<div class="mermaid-block" data-mermaid-id="' + containerId + '">'
    + '<pre class="mermaid-source" style="display:none;">' + escapeHtml(mermaidCode) + '</pre>'
    + '<div class="mermaid-render" id="' + containerId + '"></div></div>';
}

function renderNodeTables(tables) {
  if (!tables || tables.length === 0) return '';
  var html = '<div class="field-label">Tables</div>';
  tables.forEach(function(tableStr) {
    var tableLines = tableStr.split('\n').filter(function(l) { return l.trim(); });
    html += renderMarkdownTable(tableLines, []);
  });
  return html;
}

async function postRenderMathAndMermaid(container) {
  if (typeof renderMathInElement === 'function') {
    renderMathInElement(container, {
      delimiters: [
        { left: '$$', right: '$$', display: true },
        { left: '$', right: '$', display: false },
        { left: '\\(', right: '\\)', display: false },
        { left: '\\[', right: '\\]', display: true }
      ],
      throwOnError: false
    });
  }
  var mermaidBlocks = container.querySelectorAll('.mermaid-block');
  for (var block of mermaidBlocks) {
    var sourceEl = block.querySelector('.mermaid-source');
    var renderEl = block.querySelector('.mermaid-render');
    if (sourceEl && renderEl && !renderEl.getAttribute('data-processed')) {
      var code = sourceEl.textContent.trim();
      if (code) {
        try {
          var id = renderEl.id || ('mermaid-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9));
          var result = await mermaid.render(id + '-svg', code);
          renderEl.innerHTML = result.svg;
          renderEl.setAttribute('data-processed', 'true');
        } catch (e) {
          renderEl.innerHTML = '<pre style="color:var(--red);font-size:11px;">Mermaid error: '
            + escapeHtml(e.message || String(e)) + '</pre>';
          renderEl.setAttribute('data-processed', 'true');
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

var _mermaidCounter = 0;
function formatContent(text, keywords, maxLen) {
  if (!text) return '';
  var t = text;
  if (maxLen > 0 && t.length > maxLen) {
    t = t.substring(0, maxLen) + '…';
  }
  var lines = t.split('\n');
  var html = '';
  var i = 0;
  while (i < lines.length) {
    var line = lines[i].trim();
    if (!line) { i++; continue; }
    // Detect mermaid block
    if (line.startsWith('```mermaid')) {
      var mermaidLines = [];
      i++;
      while (i < lines.length && lines[i].trim() !== '```') {
        mermaidLines.push(lines[i]);
        i++;
      }
      if (i < lines.length) i++;
      var mermaidCode = mermaidLines.join('\n').trim();
      if (mermaidCode) {
        _mermaidCounter++;
        var mermaidId = 'mermaid-inline-' + _mermaidCounter + '-' + Date.now();
        html += '<div class="mermaid-block" data-mermaid-id="' + mermaidId + '">'
             + '<pre class="mermaid-source" style="display:none;">' + escapeHtml(mermaidCode) + '</pre>'
             + '<div class="mermaid-render" id="' + mermaidId + '"></div></div>';
      }
      continue;
    }
    // Detect pipe table
    if (line.startsWith('|') && line.endsWith('|')) {
      var tableLines = [];
      while (i < lines.length && lines[i].trim().startsWith('|') && lines[i].trim().endsWith('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[i].trim());
        i++;
      }
      html += renderMarkdownTable(tableLines, keywords);
      continue;
    }
    // Detect HTML <table> block (from MinerU OCR output)
    if (line.toLowerCase().startsWith('<table')) {
      var tableHtml = line;
      if (!line.toLowerCase().endsWith('</table>')) {
        i++;
        while (i < lines.length) {
          tableHtml += '\n' + lines[i];
          if (lines[i].trim().toLowerCase().endsWith('</table>')) {
            i++;
            break;
          }
          i++;
        }
      } else {
        i++;
      }
      html += renderHtmlTable(tableHtml, keywords);
      continue;
    }
    // Detect block formula $$...$$
    if (line.startsWith('$$')) {
      var formulaLines = [line.substring(2)];
      if (line.endsWith('$$') && line.length > 4) {
        formulaLines = [line.substring(2, line.length - 2)];
      } else {
        i++;
        while (i < lines.length && !lines[i].trim().endsWith('$$')) {
          formulaLines.push(lines[i]);
          i++;
        }
        if (i < lines.length) {
          formulaLines.push(lines[i].trim().replace(/\$\$/g, ''));
          i++;
        }
      }
      var formula = formulaLines.join('\n').trim();
      html += '<div class="block-formula">$$' + escapeHtml(formula) + '$$</div>';
      continue;
    }
    // Regular text line
    var processed = highlightKeywords(escapeHtml(line), keywords);
    processed = renderInlineFormulas(processed);
    html += '<p class="content-para">' + processed + '</p>';
    i++;
  }
  return html;
}

function transformNode(node, depth) {
  depth = depth || 0;
  var name = node.title || node.name || 'Untitled';
  var transformed = {
    name: name,
    title: node.title || node.name,
    level: node.level != null ? node.level : depth,
    depth: depth,
    summary: node.summary || '',
    keywords: node.keywords || [],
    exam_points: node.exam_points || [],
    content: node.content || '',
    mermaid: node.mermaid || '',
    tables: node.tables || [],
    captions: node.captions || [],
    children: []
  };

  if (node.children && Array.isArray(node.children) && node.children.length > 0) {
    transformed.children = node.children.map(function(child) {
      return transformNode(child, depth + 1);
    });
  }

  return transformed;
}

function transformNodeWithPath(node, targetPath, depth) {
  depth = depth || 0;
  var name = node.title || node.name || 'Untitled';
  var isTarget = (depth === targetPath.length - 1 && name === targetPath[depth]);
  var isAncestor = (depth < targetPath.length - 1 && name === targetPath[depth]);
  var hasChildren = node.children && Array.isArray(node.children) && node.children.length > 0;

  var transformed = {
    name: name,
    title: node.title || node.name,
    level: node.level != null ? node.level : depth,
    depth: depth,
    summary: node.summary || '',
    keywords: node.keywords || [],
    exam_points: node.exam_points || [],
    content: node.content || '',
    mermaid: node.mermaid || '',
    tables: node.tables || [],
    captions: node.captions || [],
    children: []
  };

  if (hasChildren) {
    transformed.collapsed = !isAncestor;
    transformed.children = node.children.map(function(child) {
      return transformNodeWithPath(child, targetPath, depth + 1);
    });
  }

  if (isTarget) {
    transformed.itemStyle = {
      color: '#fbbf24',
      borderColor: '#fbbf24',
      borderWidth: 3,
      shadowBlur: 16,
      shadowColor: 'rgba(251, 191, 36, 0.5)'
    };
    transformed.label = {
      color: '#fbbf24',
      fontWeight: 'bold',
      fontSize: 13
    };
    transformed.symbolSize = 18;
  }

  return transformed;
}

function flattenNodes(node, path, depth) {
  depth = depth || 0;
  path = path || [];
  var nodeName = node.title || node.name || 'Untitled';
  var currentPath = path.concat([nodeName]);
  allNodes.push({ node: node, path: currentPath, depth: depth });
  if (node.children) {
    for (var i = 0; i < node.children.length; i++) {
      flattenNodes(node.children[i], currentPath, depth + 1);
    }
  }
}

// ── Spacing Slider ──
// ── Spacing Slider ──
var collapsedNodes = new Set();

function getNodeIndexMap(tree) {
  var map = {};
  var idx = 0;
  function walk(node) {
    var name = node.title || node.name || '';
    map[name] = idx;
    idx++;
    if (node.children) node.children.forEach(walk);
  }
  if (Array.isArray(tree)) tree.forEach(walk);
  else walk(tree);
  return map;
}

function initSpacingSlider() {
  var thumbH = document.getElementById('thumbH');
  var thumbV = document.getElementById('thumbV');
  var activeThumb = null;
  var startPos = { x: 0, y: 0 };
  var startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing };

  chart.on('expand', function(params) {
    if (params.data && (params.data.name || params.data.title))
      collapsedNodes.delete(params.data.name || params.data.title);
  });
  chart.on('collapse', function(params) {
    if (params.data && (params.data.name || params.data.title))
      collapsedNodes.add(params.data.name || params.data.title);
  });

  function valToPos(val) {
    return 10 + ((val - SPACING_MIN) / (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN)) * 110;
  }

  function updateThumbPositions() {
    thumbH.style.left = valToPos(widthSpacing) + 'px';
    thumbV.style.top = (120 - valToPos(heightSpacing)) + 'px';
  }

  function applySpacing() {
    if (!chart) return;
    var isHorizontal = currentLayout === 'LR' || currentLayout === 'RL';
    var sW = (widthSpacing - 100) / 100;
    var wFactor = 1 - sW;
    var sH = (heightSpacing - 100) / 100;
    var hFactor = 1 - sH;
    chart.setOption({
      series: [{
        top: Math.max(0.3, 4 * hFactor) + '%',
        left: Math.max(0.3, 8 * wFactor) + '%',
        right: Math.max(0.3, (isHorizontal ? 20 : 8) * wFactor) + '%',
        bottom: Math.max(0.3, 4 * hFactor) + '%'
      }]
    });
    if (collapsedNodes.size > 0) {
      var nodeMap = getNodeIndexMap(treeData);
      requestAnimationFrame(function() {
        collapsedNodes.forEach(function(name) {
          var idx = nodeMap[name];
          if (idx !== undefined) {
            chart.dispatchAction({ type: 'treeExpandAndCollapse', seriesIndex: 0, dataIndex: idx });
          }
        });
      });
    }
  }

  function getPos(e) {
    return { x: e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX,
             y: e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY };
  }

  thumbH.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'h'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; });
  thumbV.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'v'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; });
  thumbH.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'h'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; }, { passive: false });
  thumbV.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) { e.preventDefault(); activeThumb = 'v'; var p = getPos(e); startPos = { x: p.x, y: p.y }; startVal = { w: widthSpacing, h: heightSpacing }; }, { passive: false });

  document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
    if (!activeThumb) return;
    var p = getPos(e);
    if (activeThumb === 'h') {
      var dx = p.x - startPos.x;
      var newW = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.w + dx / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newW !== widthSpacing) { widthSpacing = newW; updateThumbPositions(); }
    } else {
      var dy = p.y - startPos.y;
      var newH = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.h - dy / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newH !== heightSpacing) { heightSpacing = newH; updateThumbPositions(); }
    }
  });

  document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
    if (activeThumb) { applySpacing(); activeThumb = null; }
  });

  document.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
    if (!activeThumb) return;
    var p = getPos(e);
    if (activeThumb === 'h') {
      var dx = p.x - startPos.x;
      var newW = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.w + dx / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newW !== widthSpacing) { widthSpacing = newW; updateThumbPositions(); }
    } else {
      var dy = p.y - startPos.y;
      var newH = Math.round(Math.max(SPACING_MIN, Math.min(SPACING_MAX, startVal.h - dy / 110 * (SPACING_MAX - SPACING_MIN))));
      if (newH !== heightSpacing) { heightSpacing = newH; updateThumbPositions(); }
    }
  }, { passive: false });

  document.addEventListener('touchend', function() {
    if (activeThumb) { applySpacing(); activeThumb = null; }
  });

  updateThumbPositions();
}

function initChart() {
  var chartContainer = document.getElementById('chart');
  if (chart) chart.dispose();
  chart = echarts.init(chartContainer, null, { renderer: 'canvas', devicePixelRatio: window.devicePixelRatio * 2 });

  document.getElementById('layoutSelect').onchange = function(e) {
    currentLayout = e.target.value;
    renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
  };
  document.getElementById('expandLevel').onchange = function(e) {
    currentExpandLevel = parseInt(e.target.value);
    renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
  };
  chart.on('click', function(params) {
    if (params.componentSubType === 'tree') {
      showNodeInfo(params.data);
    }
  });
  window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
    if (chart) chart.resize();
  });
  initSpacingSlider();
}

function getLabelPosition(layout) {
  if (layout === 'LR') return 'right';
  if (layout === 'RL') return 'left';
  if (layout === 'TB') return 'bottom';
  return 'top';
}

function getLeafLabelPosition(layout) {
  if (layout === 'LR') return 'right';
  if (layout === 'RL') return 'left';
  if (layout === 'TB') return 'bottom';
  return 'top';
}

function renderChart(layout, expandLevel, targetPath) {
  if (!chart || !treeData) return;
  var isHorizontal = layout === 'LR' || layout === 'RL';
  var ws = (widthSpacing - 100) / 20;
  var wFactor = 1 - ws * 0.7;
  var leftMargin = Math.max(0.5, 8 * wFactor);
  var rightMargin = Math.max(0.5, (isHorizontal ? 20 : 8) * wFactor);
  var hs = (heightSpacing - 100) / 20;
  var hFactor = 1 - hs * 0.7;
  var topMargin = Math.max(0.5, 4 * hFactor);
  var bottomMargin = Math.max(0.5, 4 * hFactor);

  var transformed;
  if (targetPath && targetPath.length > 0) {
    transformed = transformNodeWithPath(treeData, targetPath);
  } else {
    transformed = transformNode(treeData);
  }

  var option = {
    backgroundColor: 'transparent',
    tooltip: {
      trigger: 'item',
      triggerOn: 'mousemove',
      confine: false,
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      borderColor: 'transparent',
      borderWidth: 0,
      padding: 0,
      textStyle: { color: '#e4e4e7', fontSize: 12, lineHeight: 20 },
      extraCssText: 'white-space: normal; word-wrap: break-word; overflow-wrap: break-word;',
      formatter: function(params) {
        if (params.componentSubType !== 'tree') return '';
        var d = params.data;
        var c = getTooltipColors();
        var html = '<div style="max-width:480px;word-wrap:break-word;overflow-wrap:break-word;background:' + c.bg + ';border:1px solid ' + c.divider + ';border-radius:8px;padding:16px 20px;">';
        html += '<div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:' + c.title + ';margin-bottom:6px;">' + d.name + '</div>';

        if (d.level != null) {
          html += '<span style="font-size:10px;color:' + c.meta + ';">Level ' + d.level + '</span>';
        }

        if (d.summary) {
          html += '<div class="tooltip-summary" style="margin-top:8px;">' + formatSummary(d.summary, d.keywords, 0) + '</div>';
        }

        if (d.keywords && d.keywords.length > 0) {
          html += '<div style="margin-top:8px;">';
          html += d.keywords.map(function(k) {
            return '<span style="display:inline-block;background:' + c.keywordBg + ';color:' + c.keywordColor + ';padding:1px 6px;border-radius:3px;font-size:10px;margin:1px 2px;">' + k + '</span>';
          }).join('');
          html += '</div>';
        }

        if (d.exam_points && d.exam_points.length > 0) {
          html += '<div style="margin-top:8px;border-top:1px solid ' + c.divider + ';padding-top:6px;">';
          d.exam_points.forEach(function(ep) {
            var freqColor = ep.frequency === '高频' ? '#22c55e' : ep.frequency === '中频' ? '#eab308' : '#71717a';
            html += '<div style="font-size:11px;margin:3px 0;"><span style="color:' + freqColor + ';">' + (ep.frequency || '') + '</span> <span style="color:' + c.meta + ';">[' + (ep.type || '') + ']</span> ' + ep.point + '</div>';
          });
          html += '</div>';
        }

        if (d.captions && d.captions.length > 0) {
          html += '<div style="margin-top:6px;border-top:1px solid ' + c.divider + ';padding-top:6px;">';
          html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:' + c.meta + ';margin-bottom:4px;">CHARTS &amp; TABLES</div>';
          d.captions.forEach(function(cap) {
            html += '<div style="font-size:11px;margin:2px 0;color:' + c.body + ';"><b>' + cap.label + '</b>: ' + cap.text + '</div>';
          });
          html += '</div>';
        }

        if (d.content) {
          html += '<div class="tooltip-content" style="margin-top:6px;border-top:1px solid ' + c.divider + ';padding-top:6px;">' + formatContent(d.content, d.keywords, 0) + '</div>';
        }

        if (d.mermaid) {
          html += '<div style="margin-top:4px;font-size:10px;color:' + c.meta + ';">[Flowchart - click for details]</div>';
        }
        if (d.tables && d.tables.length > 0) {
          html += '<div style="margin-top:4px;font-size:10px;color:' + c.meta + ';">[' + d.tables.length + ' table(s) - click for details]</div>';
        }

        if (d.children && d.children.length > 0) {
          html += '<div style="margin-top:6px;font-size:10px;color:' + c.meta + ';">' + d.children.length + ' child nodes</div>';
        }

        html += '</div>';
        return html;
      }
    },
    series: [{
      type: 'tree',
      data: [transformed],
      top: topMargin + '%',
      left: leftMargin + '%',
      right: rightMargin + '%',
      bottom: bottomMargin + '%',
      orient: layout,
      symbol: 'circle',
      symbolSize: function(value, params) {
        var d = params.data;
        if (d.symbolSize) return d.symbolSize;
        var level = d.level || 0;
        if (level === 0) return [20, 20];
        if (level === 1) return [14, 14];
        if (level === 2) return [10, 10];
        return [7, 7];
      },
      initialTreeDepth: (targetPath && targetPath.length > 0) ? -1 : expandLevel,
      expandAndCollapse: true,
      animationDuration: 500,
      animationDurationUpdate: 500,
      animationEasing: 'cubicOut',
      roam: true,
      itemStyle: {
        borderWidth: 1.5,
        borderColor: function(params) {
          if (params.data.itemStyle && params.data.itemStyle.borderColor) {
            return params.data.itemStyle.borderColor;
          }
          return getNodeColor(params.data.level || 0) + '80';
        },
        color: function(params) {
          if (params.data.itemStyle && params.data.itemStyle.color) {
            return params.data.itemStyle.color;
          }
          return getNodeColor(params.data.level || 0);
        }
      },
      label: {
        position: getLabelPosition(layout),
        verticalAlign: 'middle',
        align: 'left',
        fontSize: 12,
        color: getChartLabelColor(),
        fontWeight: 500,
        formatter: function(params) {
          var d = params.data;
          var name = d.name || '';
          if (d.summary && d.summary.length > 0 && d.level > 0) {
            return '{enhanced|} ' + name;
          }
          return name;
        },
        rich: {
          enhanced: {
            backgroundColor: 'rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.3)',
            borderRadius: 3,
            width: 4,
            height: 4
          }
        }
      },
      leaves: {
        label: {
          position: getLeafLabelPosition(layout),
          verticalAlign: 'middle',
          align: 'left',
          fontSize: 11,
          color: getChartLeafLabelColor()
        }
      },
      lineStyle: {
        color: 'rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.2)',
        width: 1.5,
        curveness: 0.5
      },
      emphasis: {
        itemStyle: {
          color: '#fbbf24',
          borderColor: '#fbbf24',
          borderWidth: 2,
          shadowBlur: 12,
          shadowColor: 'rgba(251, 191, 36, 0.3)'
        },
        label: {
          color: '#fbbf24',
          fontWeight: 'bold',
          fontSize: 13
        }
      },
      edgeShape: 'curve'
    }]
  };

  chart.setOption(option, true);
}

// ── Info Panel ──

function showNodeInfo(d) {
  var panel = document.getElementById('infoPanel');
  var content = document.getElementById('infoContent');
  currentDisplayNode = d;
  var html = '<div class="node-title">' + d.name + '</div>';

  if (d.level != null) {
    html += '<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);">Level ' + d.level + '</span>';
  }

  if (d.summary) {
    html += '<div class="field-label">Summary</div>';
    html += '<div class="summary">' + formatSummary(d.summary, d.keywords, 0) + '</div>';
  }

  if (d.keywords && d.keywords.length > 0) {
    html += '<div class="field-label">Keywords</div>';
    html += '<div class="keywords">';
    html += d.keywords.map(function(k) { return '<span class="keyword-tag">' + k + '</span>'; }).join('');
    html += '</div>';
  }

  if (d.exam_points && d.exam_points.length > 0) {
    html += '<div class="field-label">Exam Points</div>';
    d.exam_points.forEach(function(ep) {
      var freqColor = ep.frequency === '高频' ? 'var(--green)' :
                       ep.frequency === '中频' ? 'var(--yellow)' : 'var(--text3)';
      html += '<div class="exam-point">' + ep.point +
        '<div class="exam-meta"><span style="color:' + freqColor + ';">' + (ep.frequency || '-') + '</span> · ' + (ep.type || '-') + '</div></div>';
    });
  }

  if (d.captions && d.captions.length > 0) {
    html += '<div class="field-label">Charts &amp; Tables</div>';
    d.captions.forEach(function(cap) {
      html += '<div class="caption-item"><b>' + cap.label + '</b>: ' + cap.text + '</div>';
    });
  }

  if (d.content && d.content.length > 0) {
    html += '<div class="field-label">Content <button class="content-edit-btn" id="contentEditBtn" onclick="enterContentEdit()">Edit</button></div>';
    html += '<div class="content-display" id="contentDisplay">' + formatContent(d.content, d.keywords, 0) + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="content-editor-wrap" id="contentEditorWrap">';
    html += '  <div class="content-edit-bar">';
    html += '    <button id="fmtBold" onclick="execFmt(\'bold\')" title="Bold (Ctrl+B)"><b>B</b></button>';
    html += '    <button id="fmtItalic" onclick="execFmt(\'italic\')" title="Italic (Ctrl+I)"><i>I</i></button>';
    html += '    <button id="fmtStrike" onclick="execFmt(\'strikethrough\')" title="Strikethrough"><s>S</s></button>';
    html += '  </div>';
    html += '  <div class="content-editable" id="contentEditable" contenteditable="true"></div>';
    html += '  <div class="content-actions">';
    html += '    <button class="btn-save" onclick="saveContentEdit()">Save</button>';
    html += '    <button class="btn-cancel" onclick="cancelContentEdit()">Cancel</button>';
    html += '  </div>';
    html += '</div>';
  }

  if (d.mermaid) {
    html += renderNodeMermaid(d.mermaid, 'info-mermaid-' + Date.now());
  }

  if (d.tables && d.tables.length > 0) {
    html += renderNodeTables(d.tables);
  }

  if (d.children && d.children.length > 0) {
    html += '<div style="margin-top:10px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);">' + d.children.length + ' child node(s)</div>';
  }

  content.innerHTML = html;
  panel.classList.add('show');
  postRenderMathAndMermaid(content);
}

function closePanel() {
  document.getElementById('infoPanel').classList.remove('show');
  currentDisplayNode = null;
}

// ── Controls ──

function fitView() {
  if (!chart) return;
  renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
}

function expandAll() {
  if (!chart) return;
  currentExpandLevel = 5;
  document.getElementById('expandLevel').value = '5';
  renderChart(currentLayout, 5);
}

function collapseAll() {
  if (!chart) return;
  currentExpandLevel = 1;
  document.getElementById('expandLevel').value = '1';
  renderChart(currentLayout, 1);
}

// ── Export ──

async function exportMindmap() {
  if (!currentTaskId) {
    showToast('No task to export');
    return;
  }
  var btn = document.getElementById('exportBtn');
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '⏳ Exporting...';

  try {
    var res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/export/${currentTaskId}`);
    if (!res.ok) {
      var errorMessage = 'Export failed';
      try {
        var err = await res.json();
        errorMessage = err.error || err.detail || errorMessage;
      } catch (_) {
        var text = await res.text().catch(function() { return ''; });
        if (text) errorMessage = text;
      }
      throw new Error(errorMessage);
    }
    var blob = await res.blob();
    var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = 'knowledge_tree_' + currentTaskId + '.zip';
    document.body.appendChild(a);
    a.click();
    document.body.removeChild(a);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    showToast('Export downloaded! Unzip to get chapters/, md/, json/, and mindmap.html.');
  } catch (err) {
    showToast('Export failed: ' + err.message);
  } finally {
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '📦 Export';
  }
}

// ── Content Editor ──

function enterContentEdit() {
  if (!currentDisplayNode) return;
  var display = document.getElementById('contentDisplay');
  var editorWrap = document.getElementById('contentEditorWrap');
  var editable = document.getElementById('contentEditable');
  var btn = document.getElementById('contentEditBtn');

  var raw = currentDisplayNode.content || '';
  editable.innerHTML = raw.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/\n/g, '<br>');

  display.classList.add('hidden');
  editorWrap.classList.add('active');
  btn.style.display = 'none';
  editable.focus();
}

function cancelContentEdit() {
  var display = document.getElementById('contentDisplay');
  var editorWrap = document.getElementById('contentEditorWrap');
  var btn = document.getElementById('contentEditBtn');

  editorWrap.classList.remove('active');
  display.classList.remove('hidden');
  btn.style.display = '';
}

async function saveContentEdit() {
  if (!currentDisplayNode) return;
  var editable = document.getElementById('contentEditable');
  var newText = editable.innerText.trim();

  currentDisplayNode.content = newText;

  var sourceFile = currentDisplayNode._sourceFile || '';
  if (sourceFile) {
    try {
      var resp = await fetch(API_BASE + '/api/update-node', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          filename: sourceFile,
          path: currentDisplayNode._pathInFile || [],
          title: currentDisplayNode.name || currentDisplayNode.title,
          content: newText
        })
      });
      if (!resp.ok) {
        var err = await resp.json();
        console.warn('Content save failed:', err.error || resp.status);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('Content save failed:', e.message);
    }
  }

  var display = document.getElementById('contentDisplay');
  display.innerHTML = formatContent(newText, currentDisplayNode.keywords || [], 0);
  postRenderMathAndMermaid(display);
  cancelContentEdit();
}

function execFmt(command) {
  document.execCommand(command, false, null);
  document.getElementById('contentEditable').focus();
}

// ── Search ──

function toggleSearch() {
  searchExpanded = !searchExpanded;
  var panel = document.getElementById('searchPanel');
  var toggleBtn = document.getElementById('searchToggleBtn');

  if (searchExpanded) {
    panel.classList.remove('collapsed');
    toggleBtn.classList.add('shifted');
    document.getElementById('searchInput').focus();
  } else {
    panel.classList.add('collapsed');
    toggleBtn.classList.remove('shifted');
  }
}

function performSearch() {
  var input = document.getElementById('searchInput');
  var query = input.value.trim();
  var clearBtn = document.getElementById('searchClearBtn');
  var resultsEl = document.getElementById('searchResults');
  var statusEl = document.getElementById('searchStatus');

  if (!query) {
    clearBtn.style.display = 'none';
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">Type to search node titles...</div>';
    statusEl.textContent = '';
    return;
  }

  clearBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';

  if (!allNodes || allNodes.length === 0) {
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">No tree data loaded</div>';
    statusEl.textContent = '';
    return;
  }

  var queryLower = query.toLowerCase();
  var matches = [];

  for (var i = 0; i < allNodes.length; i++) {
    var nodeData = allNodes[i];
    var title = (nodeData.node.title || nodeData.node.name || '').toLowerCase();
    if (title.indexOf(queryLower) !== -1) {
      matches.push({ index: i, node: nodeData.node, path: nodeData.path });
    }
  }

  if (matches.length === 0) {
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">No matching nodes found</div>';
    statusEl.textContent = '';
    return;
  }

  statusEl.textContent = matches.length + ' node(s) found';

  var html = '';
  for (var m = 0; m < matches.length; m++) {
    var match = matches[m];
    var pathHtml = '';
    for (var p = 0; p < match.path.length; p++) {
      if (p > 0) pathHtml += '<span class="path-sep">&#9654;</span>';
      pathHtml += escapeHtml(match.path[p] || '');
    }

    var title = match.node.title || match.node.name || '';
    var titleLower = title.toLowerCase();
    var queryLen = query.length;
    var titleHtml = '';
    var lastIdx = 0;
    var idx = titleLower.indexOf(queryLower);
    while (idx !== -1) {
      titleHtml += escapeHtml(title.substring(lastIdx, idx));
      titleHtml += '<span class="search-highlight">' + escapeHtml(title.substring(idx, idx + queryLen)) + '</span>';
      lastIdx = idx + queryLen;
      idx = titleLower.indexOf(queryLower, lastIdx);
    }
    titleHtml += escapeHtml(title.substring(lastIdx));

    html += '<div class="search-result-item" data-node-index="' + match.index + '" onclick="expandToNode(' + match.index + ')">';
    html += '<div class="search-result-path">' + pathHtml + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="search-result-title">' + titleHtml + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
  }

  resultsEl.innerHTML = html;
}

function expandToNode(nodeIndex) {
  if (!chart || !treeData || nodeIndex >= allNodes.length) return;

  var targetPath = allNodes[nodeIndex].path;

  // Ensure search panel stays open and mark active
  var items = document.querySelectorAll('.search-result-item');
  for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
    items[i].classList.remove('active');
  }
  var activeItem = document.querySelector('.search-result-item[data-node-index="' + nodeIndex + '"]');
  if (activeItem) activeItem.classList.add('active');

  renderChart(currentLayout, -1, targetPath);
}

function clearSearch() {
  document.getElementById('searchInput').value = '';
  document.getElementById('searchClearBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('searchResults').innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">Type to search node titles...</div>';
  document.getElementById('searchStatus').textContent = '';
  if (chart && treeData) {
    renderChart(currentLayout, currentExpandLevel);
  }
}

// Ctrl+F to open search, Escape to close
document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
  if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'f') {
    if (treeData) {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (!searchExpanded) toggleSearch();
      document.getElementById('searchInput').focus();
      document.getElementById('searchInput').select();
    }
  }
  if (e.key === 'Escape' && searchExpanded) {
    toggleSearch();
  }
});

// ── Zoom Slider ──
var currentZoom = 1;
function updateZoom(zoom) {
  currentZoom = zoom;
  var container = document.getElementById('chart');
  container.style.transform = 'scale(' + zoom + ')';
  container.style.transformOrigin = 'center center';
  container.style.transition = 'transform 0.15s ease';
  document.getElementById('zoomLabel').textContent = Math.round(zoom * 100) + '%';
  document.getElementById('zoomRange').value = Math.round(zoom * 100);
}
document.getElementById('zoomRange').addEventListener('input', function(e) {
  updateZoom(parseInt(e.target.value) / 100);
});

// ── Helpers ──

function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise(function(resolve) { setTimeout(resolve, ms); });
}

function showToast(msg) {
  var toast = document.getElementById('toast');
  toast.innerHTML = msg.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
  toast.classList.add('show');
  setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.remove('show'); }, 5000);
}

</html>

import subprocess
import webbrowser
import time
import sys
import os

HOST = os.environ.get("HOST", "0.0.0.0")
PORT = os.environ.get("PORT", "8000")
URL = f"http://localhost:{PORT}"

print(f"正在启动 KnowledgeTree 服务...")
proc = subprocess.Popen(
    [sys.executable, "-m", "uvicorn", "knowledge-compiler.server:app", "--host", HOST, "--port", PORT],
    cwd=os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)),
)

time.sleep(2)
print(f"服务已启动，正在打开浏览器: {URL}")
webbrowser.open(URL)

try:
    proc.wait()
except KeyboardInterrupt:
    print("\n正在关闭服务...")
    proc.terminate()
    proc.wait()
    print("已关闭。")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Advanced test: Word document processing and LLM structuring.
"""

import sys
import os
import json
import tempfile
from pathlib import Path

COMPILER_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'knowledge-compiler')
sys.path.insert(0, COMPILER_DIR)


def test_word_processing():
    """Test Word document extraction to markdown."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Word Document Processing")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    try:
        from docx import Document
        from parser.text_extractor import docx_to_markdown
        
        # Create a test Word document
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix='.docx', delete=False) as tmp:
            doc = Document()
            
            # Add content with different heading styles
            h1 = doc.add_heading('第一章 教育学基础', level=1)
            doc.add_paragraph('教育学是研究教育现象和教育规律的科学。')
            
            h2 = doc.add_heading('第一节 教育的定义', level=2)
            doc.add_paragraph('教育是指有目的、有计划、有组织地对受教育者进行思想、品德、知识和技能的培养。')
            
            h3 = doc.add_heading('知识点1：教育的本质', level=3)
            doc.add_paragraph('教育的本质是一种社会现象。')
            
            # Add a table
            table = doc.add_table(rows=2, cols=2)
            table.rows[0].cells[0].text = '概念'
            table.rows[0].cells[1].text = '定义'
            table.rows[1].cells[0].text = '教育'
            table.rows[1].cells[1].text = '有计划的培养'
            
            docx_path = tmp.name
            doc.save(docx_path)
        
        # Test extraction
        markdown = docx_to_markdown(docx_path)
        
        print(f"✓ Word document created and extracted")
        print(f"✓ Extracted {len(markdown)} characters")
        
        # Verify key content
        checks = [
            ("# 第一章 教育学基础" in markdown, "Level-1 heading"),
            ("## 第一节 教育的定义" in markdown, "Level-2 heading"),
            ("### 知识点1：教育的本质" in markdown, "Level-3 heading"),
            ("教育的本质是一种社会现象" in markdown, "Paragraph content"),
            ("|" in markdown, "Table format"),
        ]
        
        all_passed = True
        for check, desc in checks:
            status = "✓" if check else "✗"
            print(f"{status} {desc}")
            if not check:
                all_passed = False
        
        os.unlink(docx_path)
        return all_passed
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ Word processing test failed: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        return False


def test_unstructured_text_detection():
    """Test detection of unstructured vs structured text."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Structured vs Unstructured Text Detection")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    try:
        from parser.text_extractor import has_heading_structure
        
        structured = """# 主题一
内容一

## 子主题一
更多内容"""
        
        unstructured = """这是一段关于教育的讨论。教育是社会的重要组成部分。
        
教师的作用很重要。他们需要掌握学科知识和教学技能。
        
学生应该主动学习。这样才能取得好成绩。"""
        
        structured_check = has_heading_structure(structured)
        unstructured_check = has_heading_structure(unstructured)
        
        print(f"✓ Structured text detected as: {structured_check} (expected True)")
        print(f"✓ Unstructured text detected as: {unstructured_check} (expected False)")
        
        return structured_check and not unstructured_check
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ Detection test failed: {e}")
        return False


def test_context_bridging_metadata():
    """Test that context bridging metadata is correctly set."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Context Bridging Metadata Validation")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    try:
        from parser.text_extractor import split_large_text
        
        # Create a multi-section text that will be split
        text = """# 第一章 教育学基础

第一章的内容很多。 """ * 50  # Repeat to make it large
        
        chunks = split_large_text(text, max_chars=1000)
        
        print(f"✓ Text split into {len(chunks)} chunks")
        
        # Validate metadata
        issues = []
        for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
            # Check all required fields
            required_fields = ['text', 'index', 'total', 'is_first', 'is_last']
            for field in required_fields:
                if field not in chunk:
                    issues.append(f"Chunk {i} missing field: {field}")
            
            # Check consistency
            if chunk['index'] != i:
                issues.append(f"Chunk {i} has wrong index: {chunk['index']}")
            if chunk['total'] != len(chunks):
                issues.append(f"Chunk {i} has wrong total: {chunk['total']}")
            
            # Check first/last flags
            if i == 0 and not chunk['is_first']:
                issues.append(f"Chunk 0 should be marked first")
            if i == len(chunks) - 1 and not chunk['is_last']:
                issues.append(f"Last chunk should be marked last")
        
        if not issues:
            print("✓ All metadata fields present and correct")
            for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
                print(f"  Chunk {i}: {len(chunk['text'])} chars, "
                      f"first={chunk['is_first']}, last={chunk['is_last']}")
            return True
        else:
            for issue in issues:
                print(f"✗ {issue}")
            return False
            
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ Metadata test failed: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        return False


def test_fallback_tree_generation():
    """Test fallback tree generation when LLM is unavailable."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: Fallback Tree Generation")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    try:
        from parser.llm_structurer import _fallback_tree
        
        chunk = {
            "text": """这是一个无结构的文本片段。

第一段内容很重要。我们需要理解其中的概念。

第二段介绍具体的方法。这些方法经过验证。

第三段总结要点。记住这些关键信息。""",
            "index": 0,
            "total": 1,
            "is_first": True,
            "is_last": True,
        }
        
        tree = _fallback_tree(chunk)
        
        print(f"✓ Fallback tree generated")
        print(f"✓ Root title: {tree.get('title')}")
        print(f"✓ Children count: {len(tree.get('children', []))}")
        
        # Validate structure
        if tree.get('children'):
            print("✓ Tree has children nodes")
            for i, child in enumerate(tree['children'][:3]):
                print(f"  - {child.get('title', 'Untitled')[:50]}")
            return True
        else:
            print("✗ Tree has no children")
            return False
            
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ Fallback tree test failed: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        return False

            else:
                print(f"  - Processing strategy: Direct markdown parsing")
        
        return True
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ Pipeline test failed: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        return False


def test_file_upload_scenario():
    """Simulate the file upload scenario."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST: File Upload Scenario")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    try:
        from server import detect_file_type, sanitize_filename
        
        test_files = [
            "教育学原理.docx",
            "学习笔记.txt",
            "课程讲义.pdf",
        ]
        
        for filename in test_files:
            file_type = detect_file_type(filename)
            safe_name = sanitize_filename(filename)
            
            type_label = {"pdf": "PDF", "word": "Word", "text": "TXT"}.get(file_type, file_type)
            
            print(f"✓ {filename}")
            print(f"  - Detected as: {type_label}")
            print(f"  - Safe filename: {safe_name}")
            
            if file_type == "word":
                print(f"  - Will process: docx_to_markdown() → split_large_text()")
            elif file_type == "text":
                print(f"  - Will process: txt_to_markdown() → split_large_text()")
            elif file_type == "pdf":
                print(f"  - Will process: PDF split → MinerU OCR → markdown")
        
        return True
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ Upload scenario test failed: {e}")
        return False


def main():
    """Run all advanced tests."""
    print("\n")
    print("╔" + "=" * 58 + "╗")
    print("║" + " ADVANCED DOCUMENT PROCESSING TESTS ".center(58) + "║")
    print("╚" + "=" * 58 + "╝")
    
    tests = [
        ("Word Document Processing", test_word_processing),
        ("Structured/Unstructured Detection", test_unstructured_text_detection),
        ("Context Bridging Metadata", test_context_bridging_metadata),
        ("Fallback Tree Generation", test_fallback_tree_generation),
        ("Pipeline Flow with Mock Units", test_pipeline_with_mock_units),
        ("File Upload Scenario", test_file_upload_scenario),
    ]
    
    results = {}
    for test_name, test_func in tests:
        try:
            results[test_name] = test_func()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"\n✗ Test '{test_name}' crashed: {e}")
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            results[test_name] = False
    
    # Summary
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("ADVANCED TESTS SUMMARY")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    passed = sum(1 for v in results.values() if v)
    total = len(results)
    
    for test_name, result in results.items():
        status = "PASS ✓" if result else "FAIL ✗"
        print(f"{status}: {test_name}")
    
    print(f"\nTotal: {passed}/{total} tests passed")
    
    if passed == total:
        print("\n✓ All advanced tests passed!")
        return 0
    else:
        print(f"\n⚠ {total - passed} test(s) had issues.")
        return 1


if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

"""

        ("document.docx", "word"),

        if result != expected:

    return all_passed

教育是什么？教育是人类社会的一种重要现象，是社会文明的重要组成部分。

第一节 教育的定义

教育是指有目的、有计划、有组织地对受教育者进行思想、品德、知识和技能的培养。

知识点1 教育的属性

教育具有社会性、历史性和阶级性。

知识点2 教育的功能

教育具有培养人、传承文明、发展社会的功能。

第二节 教育的发展

教育随着社会的发展而发展，不同的社会形式有不同的教育形式。""")

            return False
        
        return True
    finally:
        os.unlink(txt_path)


def test_large_text_splitting():
    """Test automatic text splitting for large documents."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 4: Large Text Splitting with Context Bridging")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    from parser.text_extractor import split_large_text
    
    # Create a large text with multiple sections
    large_text = """# 第一章 教育学基础

## 第一节 教育的定义

教育是人类社会的一种重要现象，是指有目的、有计划、有组织地对受教育者进行思想、品德、知识和技能的培养和训练。

### 知识点1：教育的本质

教育的本质是一种社会现象，它是社会文明传承的重要方式。教育既是社会发展的产物，也是推动社会进步的重要力量。

### 知识点2：教育的主要特征

教育具有目的性、计划性、组织性和系统性。

## 第二节 教育的功能

教育的功能是多方面的，包括人才培养功能、文化传承功能、社会发展功能等。

### 知识点3：人才培养功能

人才培养是教育的首要功能，教育通过培养各种类型的人才来满足社会需要。

### 知识点4：文化传承功能

教育是文化传承的重要途径，通过教育可以将人类文明积累代代相传。

# 第二章 教育的历史发展

## 第一节 古代教育

古代教育主要以私塾和官学的形式存在，教育内容主要是儒家经典和其他传统知识。

## 第二节 近代教育

近代教育是指从鸦片战争到1949年中华人民共和国成立这一历史时期的教育。

## 第三节 现代教育

现代教育是指1949年以来的教育，包括探索阶段、建设阶段和改革阶段。
""" * 2  # Repeat to make it larger
    
    # Test default splitting
    chunks = split_large_text(large_text, max_chars=2000)
    
    print(f"✓ Text split into {len(chunks)} chunks")
    
    # Verify chunk metadata
    all_correct = True
    for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
        if chunk['index'] != i:
            print(f"✗ Chunk {i}: index mismatch ({chunk['index']})")
            all_correct = False
        if chunk['total'] != len(chunks):
            print(f"✗ Chunk {i}: total mismatch ({chunk['total']} vs {len(chunks)})")
            all_correct = False
        if i == 0 and not chunk['is_first']:
            print(f"✗ Chunk {i}: should be marked as first")
            all_correct = False
        if i == len(chunks) - 1 and not chunk['is_last']:
            print(f"✗ Chunk {i}: should be marked as last")
            all_correct = False
    
    if all_correct:
        print("✓ Context bridging metadata: OK")
        for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
            print(f"  Chunk {i}: {len(chunk['text'])} chars, "
                  f"first={chunk['is_first']}, last={chunk['is_last']}")
    
    return all_correct


def test_heading_detection():
    """Test heading structure detection."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 5: Heading Structure Detection")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    from parser.text_extractor import has_heading_structure
    
    test_cases = [
        ("# 标题1\n## 标题2\n内容", True, "Multiple headings"),
        ("# 标题\n内容", True, "Single heading"),
        ("无标题内容\n更多内容\n还有内容", False, "No headings"),
        ("", False, "Empty text"),
    ]
    
    all_correct = True
    for text, expected, desc in test_cases:
        result = has_heading_structure(text)
        status = "✓" if result == expected else "✗"
        print(f"{status} {desc}: {result} (expected {expected})")
        if result != expected:
            all_correct = False
    
    return all_correct


def test_pipeline_integration():
    """Test the complete pipeline with mock data."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 6: Pipeline Integration")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # Check if all pipeline functions are accessible
    try:
        from server import (
            detect_file_type,
            _prepare_text_units,
        )
        from parser.text_extractor import split_large_text, has_heading_structure
        from parser.llm_structurer import structure_all_chunks
        
        print("✓ All pipeline functions imported successfully")
        
        # Test LLM structurer import path
        import httpx
        print("✓ httpx dependency available")
        
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ Pipeline integration test failed: {e}")
        return False


def test_dependencies():
    """Test that all required dependencies are installed."""
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("TEST 7: Dependencies Check")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    required_deps = [
        ('fastapi', 'FastAPI'),
        ('httpx', 'httpx'),
        ('docx', 'python-docx'),
        ('chardet', 'chardet'),
    ]
    
    all_present = True
    for module_name, package_name in required_deps:
        try:
            __import__(module_name)
            print(f"✓ {package_name}: installed")
        except ImportError:
            print(f"✗ {package_name}: NOT installed")
            print(f"  Install with: pip install {package_name}")
            all_present = False
    
    return all_present


def main():
    """Run all tests."""
    print("\n")
    print("╔" + "=" * 58 + "╗")
    print("║" + " DOCUMENT PROCESSING PIPELINE VERIFICATION ".center(58) + "║")
    print("╚" + "=" * 58 + "╝")
    
    tests = [
        ("Imports", test_imports),
        ("Dependencies", test_dependencies),
        ("File Type Detection", test_file_type_detection),
        ("Text Extraction", test_text_extraction),
        ("Large Text Splitting", test_large_text_splitting),
        ("Heading Detection", test_heading_detection),
        ("Pipeline Integration", test_pipeline_integration),
    ]
    
    results = {}
    for test_name, test_func in tests:
        try:
            results[test_name] = test_func()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"\n✗ Test '{test_name}' crashed: {e}")
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            results[test_name] = False
    
    # Summary
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("SUMMARY")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    passed = sum(1 for v in results.values() if v)
    total = len(results)
    
    for test_name, result in results.items():
        status = "PASS ✓" if result else "FAIL ✗"
        print(f"{status}: {test_name}")
    
    print(f"\nTotal: {passed}/{total} tests passed")
    
    if passed == total:
        print("\n✓ All tests passed! Pipeline is ready for use.")
        return 0
    else:
        print(f"\n✗ {total - passed} test(s) failed. Please review above.")
        return 1


if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())
